Chapter 3400 Rock Giants The intersecting stalagmites pressed heavily from all directions. The five Ear Mice squeaked as the passageway closed.

One of the Ear Mice took out its Other Shore Token, an iron house.

"Everyone, get in the house! Hurry up! Take cover!"

Such tokens of descending type were rare and unpopular on the Other Shore. This token could be used to imprison opponents. It could also be used as a defensive shield due to its durability.

Without hesitation, the other four Ear Mice sought refuge.

Crack! Crack! Crack! The stalagmites extended rapidly until they were pushing at the surface of the iron house.

Clank! Clank! Clank! Under the great pressure, the iron house made a grating sound.

"The iron house can resist three thousand divine megatons of force. The stalagmites are heavy, but they are not enough to break it! Don't worry!" the first Ear Mouse said.

"Squeak! Squeak! Squeak!"

"Squeak! Squeak! Squeak!"

The other four Ear Mice echoed.

In terms of cultivation methods and theurgies, the Ear Mice were weaker than the other super forces, but their Other Shore Tokens had always been the strongest.

But the relief didn't last long. After a few seconds, the foundations of the iron house couldn't bear the load any longer. It was crushed by the great force.

Bang! The five Ear Mice in the iron house were crushed into minced meat in the blink of an eye.

The stalagmites in the cave continued to grow rapidly. Even though the group had passed through the narrow place, they still couldn't afford to stop running.

"Speed up! You can't resist these stalagmites," Zen reminded.

Zen had tried to prevent the growth of those stalagmites, but even he couldn't restrain the power contained within them.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! They all silently rushed onward.

The stalagmites grew faster and faster. From time to time, some even shot out from the flanks. Any carelessness would cause death.

Through this, the advantage of the Ear Mice was revealed.

They were small and flexible. Even if a stalagmite suddenly shot down from above, they could easily dodge it.

Sally had never experienced such danger. Her round eyes wide open, she kept flying up and down. Suddenly, a stalagmite shot down from above. It was as sharp as a sword, and it was indestructible.

Anyone hit by it would feel like they were being stabbed with thousands of divine megatons of force, except excruciatingly slower.

The stalagmite shot out toward Sally's head.

"Look out!"

Chaim, who was flying on the right, knocked Sally aside, pushing her a few feet away.

Just like Zen, Chaim paid attention to everyone while flying, but he cared about Sally the most.

Crack! The stalagmite missed Sally, but it pierced Chaim's right shoulder. He had tried to avoid it but failed. His muscles cut by the stalagmite, he bled profusely.

"Chaim, you..." Sally was shocked to see Chaim's large wound.

"Don't space out! Keep running!" Chaim shouted in a loud voice.

The stalagmites in the cave grew more and more quickly. There was no time to waste.

After tens of thousands of feet, the stalagmites finally stopped shooting out.

Everyone had passed through in peace.

Hutton and the others gasped for air.

Sally cleaned the wound on Chaim's shoulder.

Darth and the other Ear Mice looked back with lingering fear. The passageway they had come through was now crammed with stalagmites.

Zen looked back at the stalagmites and walked toward them.

"Zen, what are you doing?" Dorothy asked.

"I want to check them out. They are too strange," Zen replied.

No less than a million stalagmites had grown along the way. If each of them needed a Chaotic Source Spirit to support it, then there must be over a million Chaotic Source Spirits. But this was obviously impossible.

Zen approached the stalagmites. He lightly touched one of them, poking a hole right through it.

"Sure enough," Zen muttered.

"The stalagmites have become fragile," said Darth, agape.

"Yes." Zen nodded as he raised his head to look at the cave ceiling. "The Chaotic Source Spirits came all the way with us. They stayed in the stalagmites and used them to attack us."

"They must have kept moving ahead of us to merge with new stalagmites, abandoning the ones we've already passed," Darth remarked. "The Chaotic Source Spirits moved fast through these rocks!"

Zen didn't care about this. He narrowed his eyes. "So why have they given up now?"

"What do you mean?" Darth was puzzled by Zen's words.

Zen turned to look at the deep passage ahead. "If there is an end to the cave, the Chaotic Source Spirits just need to wait there to make sure we can't break through quickly. Then the other Chaotic Source Spirits can use the stalagmites to assassinate us. Since we can't use the Grand Teleportation, we would surely die."

After Zen finished his words, a chill went through his companions.

No one would be able to escape such a maneuver, if true.

"Master Zen, don't give them ideas! The Chaotic Source Spirits are intelligent and they can understand human language!" said Darth anxiously.

Zen smiled calmly. "Precisely because they are intelligent, they must have already thought of this. The only reason why they didn't push through it is they have other ways to deal with us, and they are confident that they can capture us."

With these words, Zen pointed forward.

Rocks in the distance started to move. They separated from the walls and turned into rock giants.

An ordinary rock giant wouldn't have been a threat. But those possessed by the Chaotic Source Spirits were indestructible.

Dong! Dong! Dong! Huge rock giants emerged from all directions and charged toward the group.

Seeing this, Dorothy, Elvinia, Chaim, and the Ear Mice scrambled to take out their Other Shore Tokens.

A flower spun above Dorothy and took her shape. This was the unique Twin Blossoms. The two Dorothies, hearts connected, both carried a sword. The power of Dorothy's Origin Swordsmanship would thus be twice as strong.

The Warrior of the Stone Hill floated in the air beside Elvinia, with a sword in one hand and a thousand swords in the other.

Chaim also deployed his Other Shore Token.

Strong warriors like them were not afraid of fighting head-on. What they feared most were ambush attacks in the dark. But now that the Chaotic Source Spirits had decided to confront them face-to-face, they would definitely fight to the end.

Chapter 3401 Huge Eye Even though the ground shook as a rock giant rushed quickly towards Zen, he still remained composed and nonchalant.

The rock giant balled its huge fists and then smashed them towards Zen, but he disappeared in a flash from the spot! The next moment, he reappeared behind the rock giant.

With a crisp sound, he slashed his sword across the giant's body, but it failed to damage even the surface of the rock.

Still, Zen wasn't disappointed.

In fact, he was surprised â€” it just proved that there really was a Chaotic Source Spirit that hid inside the rock giant and strengthened its body.

Of course, he did not forget that their trip's main objective was to obtain the Chaotic Source Spirits! "Clang!"

There was a deafening crash when the rock giant stretched its arms and fell on its back.

The way it moved wasn't particularly slow, but it still couldn't touch Zen at all.

Meanwhile, Zen moved as swiftly as a light feather that glided in the wind, that even a small force could blow him away, but not damage him.

He ducked to avoid the rock giant's attack, then squinted his right eye which flashed a white beam of light.

"Authentic Visual World!"

As he employed the skill, the whole world became unusually clear in his vision. It didn't take him much effort to find several cracks on the surface of the rock giant.

"Sword Texture Technique! Break it!"

Next, he raised his sword and pointed it at the junction of two cracks found on the giant's waist.

The queen ant he had fought before had absorbed many Chaotic Source Spirits over a long period of time, so its body had only one flaw.

On the other hand, the rock giant had many flaws since it was only a temporary product.

The next events all went by in a blur.

As soon as Zen's sword touched the rock giant's weak spot, its body exploded into smithereens.

Yet, Zen didn't lower his guard even when the rock giant was now crushed into pieces.

That was because he suspected that the Chaotic Source Spirits must have been plotting something because they gathered in the main peak. Since they hadn't assassinated him with the stalagmites, he expected them to use more powerful means against him. The rock giants, however, were much weaker than he had imagined.

The thought quickly flashed in his mind â€” but no matter what the truth was, he believed that they must be able to obtain some Chaotic Source Spirits from the rock giants.

Just as the stone fragments collapsed on the ground, a small red creature emerged out of them. Compared to the ordinary Chaotic Source Spirits that Zen had seen before, this one was in a strange red color, and its big eyes were filled with ferocity instead of the loveliness the other Chaotic Source Spirits possessed.

"There's only one Chaotic Source Spirit?" he muttered. His eyes suddenly lit up in realization. Still, he stretched out his hand and an invisible force enveloped the little creature.

To his surprise, the little creature moved unimaginably fast. It directly plunged into the ground in an attempt to escape.

But, Zen wouldn't allow his prey to escape before him.

At that moment, the force he had just released turned into an invisible giant claw and grasped at the ground.

The Chaotic Source Spirit was extremely exhausted. Even if it merged with the rocks again, it wouldn't be able to make them solid to resist Zen.

The rocks were as fragile as bean curd under the pressure of the invisible giant claw. With just a slight effort, the giant claw lifted them off the ground together with the Chaotic Source Spirit that hid inside them.

At that moment, the rocks suddenly exploded in the air.

The Chaotic Source Spirit immediately escaped and went straight towards Zen! It came to an abrupt halt as its little red body swelled rapidly and shattered into pieces.

Zen couldn't believe it. Trapped in a desperate situation, it decided to blow itself up! Fortunately, the blast wasn't enough to cause any damage to him. He just covered his face with his hand and easily blocked the suicide attack.

After the slight explosion, he heard a small clank by his feet.

It turned out to be an amber crystal that fell on the ground.

Zen picked it up as he glanced across the surrounding battlefield.

Generally speaking, the rock giants weren't considered as formidable enemies. Elvinia, Dorothy, Hutton, Sally, Chaim, and the Ear Mice had each fought against a rock giant. Although their own battles didn't end as fast as Zen's, the Chaotic Source Spirits inside the rock giants they faced were quickly worn out. Eventually, the rock giants became very weak.

A loud thud resounded throughout the area as the Iridescent Stone had pierced one of the rock giants.

The red Chaotic Source Spirit inside the rocks was forced out of them. As Sally gently flicked her fingers, the Iridescent Stone went back and hit the Chaotic Source Spirit, thus reducing it into pieces. Only an amber crystal remained, which dropped to the ground.

"Perfect!" Sally exclaimed with a satisfied smile.

She kicked the debris and dirt off her feet and happily picked up the amber crystal from the ground.

Although it was only one Chaotic Source Spirit, it was a reward she had reaped with her own strength.

Following her victory, several more loud bangs echoed in the field.

The other rock giants were defeated one by one, and each of them had obtained a Chaotic Source Spirit.

Once they had cleared the battlefield and gathered together, Chaim looked as if something bothered him. "I don't see the point of those strange Chaotic Source Spirits," he said.

It was known that the Chaotic Source Spirits needed to merge with each other to become powerful.

For instance, one hundred Chaotic Source Spirits that had fused together was as powerful as one Chaotic Source Realm warrior.

Thus, a thousand or even ten thousand of them merged together would have an incomparable amount of strength.

Today, however, they oddly chose to fight alone â€” which was like a free gift for Zen and his group of warriors.

"There must be something wrong with them," Zen remarked. "I have a strange feeling that something has been staring at me in the darkness in this weird place," he added with a frown.

Darth unexpectedly nodded and said, "Yes. In fact, we noticed it as soon as we got here, but we had no way to confirm our assumption."

"Exactly!" the other Ear Mice chimed in as well. One aspect of the Ear Mice's abilities was far stronger than that of humans, and that was their keen perception.

If Zen had noticed the strangeness, then the Ear Mice had surely managed to do so as well.

As a matter of fact, Zen and his companions weren't the only ones who had encountered such weird matters.

A cool, gentle breeze swept through another passageway. Yan's dress rustled elegantly against the floor as she pressed her fingers on her forehead.

She gazed at several rock giants in front of her and said in a low voice, "Break!"

The ground trembled and an audible crash was heard when the rock giants fell apart before her.

"Freeze!"

Yan opened her mouth once again, and an invisible power instantly restrained the Chaotic Source Spirits inside the rock giants.

When the little creatures were exposed, they just stared at her with hatred before they detonated themselves.

Several explosions later, all of them had turned into shreds.

There was a trace of pity and sadness in Yan's eyes as she looked at them, even though she didn't directly kill them.

She had already had a thorough understanding of these miserable creatures.

All warriors in the Other Shore Realm needed to capture the Chaotic Source Spirits in order to obtain greater power.

Although she could choose not to kill these creatures straight, they would still die at some point after the crystals had been taken out of their bodies. A moment of mercy wouldn't change the inevitable.

The Chaotic Source Spirits had a life that entailed the constant tragedy of being nurtured and slaughtered. Perhaps no other creatures could have a more miserable fate than them.

That was why the sight of hostility in their eyes made Yan uncomfortable and guilty.

In any case, that same form of slaughter had been taking place in the other passages as well.

The warriors had all reaped their first harvest in the main peak, but a dozen Chaotic Source Spirits were far from enough for them.

Meanwhile, a huge eye that resided in the main peak had been observing everything that had happened below it through the thick layers of rocks.

This huge eye was ten feet wide. Half of it flashed with a white light, and the other half with a red light. It obviously didn't belong to the Chaotic Source World, because it was an Other Shore Token.

Chapter 3402 The Eligible Targets It had been a while since the huge eye was silently observing the events below it, to embed every living creature in the main peak to its vision.

A huge ball rested under this eye, which was actually a big and powerful Chaotic Source Spirit. It measured more than a hundred feet in size, different from an ordinary one of its kind. This large ball was clearly the mother of all the Chaotic Source Spirits.

The voice of the mother of Chaotic Source Spirits broke the silence in the air. "Have you found the eligible targets?"

The huge eye flashed and sent out a part of its consciousness in response.

The eye had no organs to speak, so it could only send messages through its consciousness.

"I have many qualified targets in mind now," said the huge eye.

"Let me see!" the mother demanded. Red and white lights inside the huge eye descended in front of the mother and drew a graceful figure.

It was Yan, who wore a long dress.

The light figure showed that she was climbing up the cave, leading the members of the Snake Goddess race.

"This is a human girl who cultivates the Truth of Holy Words. She has the blood of the Snake Goddess," the huge eye explained.

The mother nodded, then started to count, "One."

Buzzâ€¦ The red and white lights flashed again and revealed another figure.

This time, it was a white-haired young man. It was none other than Khalid from the Bearing race.

"A man of the Bearing race, who cultivates the Truth of Five Orientations, owns the Five-Orientation Body, and is one of the inheritors of the Yellow Thearch."

"Two," the mother said with a blank expression.

"Buzz..."

The lights flashed some more and showed the top masters of the minor races, and the huge eye had been targeting all of them.

"There are eleven in total. What about the targets for yourself?" asked the mother.

The eye smiled. "Me? Well... I am interested in this guy."

"Buzz..."

The huge eye flashed and Zen's figure appeared, which was outlined by red and white lights.

"Is he also one of the human race? Why did you choose him?" the mother asked and looked at Zen in curiosity.

"This man is very interesting. He has merged with something of my kind,"

said the giant eye with its consciousness.

The mother was visibly shocked at this news, "You mean he has merged with an Eye of Will?"

"Yes. If I'm not mistaken, he must have assimilated an Eye of Will when he was in the Sacred Mallow Temple!" the huge eye answered affirmatively.

The mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits, however, was not interested in the giant eye's chosen target. Instead she asked, "Are you sure that we can escape safely after we possess their bodies? There are supreme masters who stay outside the Chaotic Source World. I can sense them," the mother said anxiously.

"Hmph, it's just Human Sovereign who's on guard outside. I'm afraid he can't keep us here if he is alone!" It seemed that there was a hint of contempt in the huge eye's words.

"That's good," the mother hissed. She turned to look at the phantoms of the eligible targets, and the hatred in her only grew even more. "We Chaotic Source Spirits have been kept in this place, while they slaughter and trample us at will. Now, it's time for them to pay the price and have a taste of this kind of life! You bastards want to absorb us? Let's see if you are qualified first!"

Normally, creatures of the Other Shore could not enter the Source World.

Yet, the Chaotic Source Spirit itself was quite special. After the Snake Goddess had discovered it, their pack had been nurtured carefully and grew to a great number.

Over the years, the Chaotic Source Spirits had helped nurture countless masters in the Source World.

Despite such a deed, life in the Source World was cruel for them.

Their true bodies were locked in the powerful Chaotic Source Sea on Stage Twenty-two. They couldn't even move in the slightest--but as a kind of Other Shore Token, they descended in the Chaotic Source World.

If it hadn't been for the accident a few years ago, then Chaotic Source Spirits would have been enslaved and kept in captivity for more generations.

During that time, one powerful master had killed the guardian of the Chaotic Source Sea and freed all the Chaotic Source Spirits.

The mother was the core of the Chaotic Source Spirits. She wanted to bring all the Chaotic Source Spirits back to the Other Shore and stop them from being the Other Shore Tokens for good. She wanted to end their miserable lives.

However, the master who had saved them refused the mother's request and asked the Chaotic Source Spirits to maintain what they had been doing.

The mother was confused, until a huge eye--the Dreaded Eye Demon, appeared.

To descend in the Source World, creatures of the Other Shore required some warriors to support them, or in other words, they needed a complete inner world for support. Thus, the mother was very curious as to how the Dreaded Eye Demon had broken through the Other Shore's restrictions and arrived at where they were now.

In addition, the Dreaded Eye Demon brought a task for them when it came- -to devour the top talents in the Source World.

Needless to say, the Chaotic Source Spirits were very excited when they heard the news.

Those damned creatures had devoured them for so long, and finally there was a day that they could devour them back. It was what the Chaotic Source Spirits had been dreaming of doing, but they couldn't do so, until the huge eye had arrived.

The Chaotic Source Spirits didn't have the ability to bite back, but the giant eye could. It turned out that the master who had freed them had already found the escape route in advance.

It was usually the mother's strategy to spread the plenty of Chaotic Source Spirits across the four peaks in the north, east, west, and south, in order to protect as many of them as possible.

As for those warriors who entered the main peak without permission, the mother would lead all the other Chaotic Source Spirits to fight back! This time, however, was different. Now, the mother took all the Chaotic Source Spirits back to the main peak so they could attract those talents to their location. The tests in the caves and passageways were nothing more than observation methods to select the best talents. At this point, the giant eye had already chosen the targets suitable for their consumption.

Below the huge eye's hideaway, creatures of various races had entered the main peak one after another. All of them encountered the same situations as Zen and the others had.

It was relatively late when the Evil God had entered the main peak.

It was known that the members of the Separate Abyss race were incomparable to those of the ordinary forces. Four members of their race had very special Other Shore Tokens. Those four relied on each other and formed a perfect circle. They were so strong that the strength they showed through the circle was enough to kill the masters at the Chaotic Source Realm.

The Evil God fought against them and although he tried his best, he had only seriously injured one of them. In the end, he had to retreat.

It was the first time that the Evil God couldn't defeat warriors who were at the same level as him! Still, the Evil God didn't care about it at all. After all, he had already killed a large number of people in the Chaotic Source World and obtained so much. What he only had to do now was to reach the Chaotic Source Realm.

Meanwhile, there were rock giants that blocked Zen and his group's path along their journey.

The rock giants didn't hinder Zen and his companions, but the warriors didn't get many Chaotic Source Spirits from them, either.

They had soon climbed a distance of twenty thousand feet up the cave, but only got a little more than ninety Chaotic Source Spirits. It was not enough for any of them when the gain was to be shared.

Yet, Zen wasn't discouraged at all.

The remaining hundreds of thousands of Chaotic Source Spirits must be hiding somewhere on the main peak, waiting for them to harvest.

After they climbed more than thirty thousand feet, they were almost in the middle of the main peak.

The Chaotic Source Spirits seemed to have hollowed out the center of the main peak, as there was a huge hole formed in the middle. As soon as they stepped into the huge cave, they all stopped walking.

There were all kinds of patterns that were engraved on the cave's walls, which made Zen and his companions feel as if they were in a huge palace.

"Look at them... What do the patterns stand for?" Sally looked around, her eyes blinking in curiosity. "I've seen these patterns before," said Chaim.

He continued, "When I was in the first stage of the Other Shore Realm..."

"They are the sculptures in the Sacred Mallow Temple." Dorothy glanced at Zen and nodded, "Me and Zen explored that temple together. I'm sure of it!"

Chapter 3403 Sculptures As Zen paced around the cave, he walked towards a corner and observed the sculptures on the walls.

The sculptures varied in forms, figures, and creatures. From cattle, to snakes, to birds. The sculptures were unique in their own ways.

Sadly, none of the sculptures was the Dreaded Eye Demon. Zen knew what he was looking for, especially since the Dreaded Eye Demon was hard to miss as it was only an eyeball. Zen had prior knowledge to them when he integrated with the Eye of Will.

"These sculptures are exactly the same as those in the Sacred Mallow Temple," Zen pointed out, nodding his head in approval.

The members and disciples of powerful forces never settled at the Stage One for long. As for Zen, he only entered the temple because some humans had invited him.

Chaim was also an exception to this. He had just entered the Other Shore, and grew curious about the place. Once, he entered the Sacred Mallow Temple, too.

"But why are all these sculptures here?" Dorothy asked, curious to know more.

She had been through a lot in the past. The first time she entered the Sacred Mallow Temple, she had struggled and was nearly killed inside.

"The risky thing in the Sacred Mallow Temple was the Soul Purifying Light, which could kill all the Souls of Light," Zen comforted her. "Good thing we don't have that here." He paused and looked back at Dorothy.

"What I don't understand is how the Chaotic Source Spirits have something to do with the Dreaded Eye Demons..."

This bothered Zen, especially because these were two completely different races.

Because he didn't have enough information, he couldn't understand. More so for the others, who had no clue about anything.

The group had made it to the end of the cave. Though there were eight other pathways around the cave, they only motioned downwards. It meant that these passages were probably connected to the other eight entrances at the bottom of the main peak.

"The Chaotic Source Spirits must be hiding up here." Elvinia nudged above.

"I'm sure that we'll find our way out if we break the cave ceiling."

The Chaotic Source Spirits had the ability to cut the rocks and moved in and out as they pleased. If it wasn't difficult for spirits, it should be possible for the group to do the same.

As Zen, Chaim and the others thought of more plans, another group of people came through another passage.

They were from the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race.

When they met eyes with Zen and his companions, their eyes widened in surprise. The silver haired young man in the lead, Khalid, was carrying a long spear on his shoulder. He squinted in arrogance.

"Interesting," muttered Khalid. "It saddened me that I didn't come cross you guys earlier. I didn't expect to see you here at all." Khalid smiled, but his kindness remained questionable. Just then, he lightly tapped on the spear, and it suddenly shook while a wisp of white light wrapped itself around the weapon.

Just as Khalid was about to make a move, another group of people appeared from another passage. They were from the New Moon race and the Divine Farmer race, and they didn't seem to be pleased either.

The man called "Mount" from the Divine Farmer race, stood at the forefront of the group. On his shoulder was a little girl named Mya, who had long, curly hair and a snarky expression.

When the two saw Zen and Elvinia, they smiled at each other in eagerness.

"Uncle Mount, are you going to fight with them right now? What a coincidence! The two people on the first row, right here, at the same time..."

Mya said this in hushed tones, keeping her expression hidden behind her curly locks of hair.

Mount narrowed his eyes and gave Zen and Elvinia a good look.

Aside from fusing with Chaotic Source Spirits, he planned to get rid of these two as well.

If they had obtained enough Chaotic Source Spirits, they would have already attacked Zen.

However, they were on the lookout for the Chaotic Source Spirits that had disappeared. They couldn't afford a delay. Also, hosting a battle in a cave was not the best course of action right now.

Mount was a steady and prudent person. He wouldn't challenge someone without full preparation.

"Let's wait a while," Mount decided. "Our main goal is still to retrieve the Chaotic Source Spirits. We can't go back empty-handed. They can live a little longer," he chuckled, drawing away from Zen and the rest.. He looked around, scanning the cave, when the strange sculptures caught his sight.

Khalid suddenly spoke up. "The Chaotic Source Spirits are surely important, but killing the good-for-nothings from the Oneness Sky Palace is proper business. If you don't want to take action against them, I'll take matters into my own hands." He was not as scrupulous nor as patient as Mount. Eagerness flashed in his eyes as his spear vibrated on his shoulder.

Hearing this, Elvinia, Dorothy, Chaim, and the rest of their group were distraught.

They knew they were outnumbered and their opponents were strong, so they were at a disadvantage.

Zen, being the leader of the group, took a step forward and calmly said, "In my opinion, generally speaking, most people who describe others as goodfor-nothings are just cowards. If you want to prove yourself so bad, you can do better than just spitting nonsense!" He let out a laugh.

Khalid, on the other hand, was not impressed with Zen at all. To Khalid, Mount, Mya, the only person they should be cautious with was the young man in black. Zen and Elvinia were nothing but prey to them.

In any case, they already ruled out the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace because they seemed too weak. They thought they would just endure all kinds of sarcasms without talking back! However, they were surprised to see Zen speak up so confidently. Khalid chuckled and said, "I'm really surprised. After so many years, the Oneness Sky Palace finally has a member with balls." He gestured towards Zen.

"Since it seems like you're eager to die, don't mind me being rude."

After he said that, he gently pulled out the white, magnificent spear from his shoulder. As the tip of the weapon swept the ground, the rocks beneath it were sliced right at the middle. This spear's sharpness was no laughing matter.

"You? Rude?" Zen raised his eyebrows, questioning this arrogant man before him. As he said so, the tip of the Snow Sword slowly stretched out from his space ring. He took hold of it and pointed it towards the members of the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race. Pleased with their reactions, he said, "This has nothing to do with manners." He looked at everyone in the eye, and then gave a wink at Khalid. "It's just, well, none of you can leave here alive."

As soon as he finished speaking, the diamond-shaped Civilization Artifact in his inner world began to move.

Once it was completely unraveled, it resembled a spiky ball.

To add, the unique aura of Regal Jade Civilization gave out in full bloom, which added to the artifact's extraordinary impression.

"You arrogant bastard!"

"You just want to die!"

"We won't hesitate to kill you!"

The members of all four races, the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race included, roared in anger.

In an instant, Khalid, Mount, Mya were smiling no longer.

They realized that they had just underestimated Zen.

After all, the young man in black who they had feared the most, was a creation of Zen's inner world.

But these people weren't going to back down now. They had been through hell and back, so they had no reason to retreat now.

Besides, they still outnumbered Zen and his companions by a large number, so they still stood with great leverage.

"Phew!"

The tension in the atmosphere thickened as a battle was just around the corner.

But just as everyone took their battle stances, footsteps echoed throughout the cave.

One more group came through another passage.

"Brother!"

The group that emerged was the Snake Goddess race, led by Yan.

They would have been the first to enter, but Yan spent too much time catching Chaotic Source Spirits, making them the last to arrive.

Seeing that Zen was safe and unharmed, Yan was more than delighted. She was relieved as she strode forward to give him a hug.

The Pear Hill had the most members, so they had the advantage of calling the shots. Though they were hit by the hurricane, they could easily gather quickly and continue moving.

Members of the Snake Goddess race and the Oneness Sky Palace gathered together, impressively outnumbering the Bearing race and the other three races altogether.

Chapter 3404 Unexpected Attack Acting on instinct, six women of the Snake Goddess race stationed themselves before Yan. They had their eyes fixated on the people of the Bearing race, and the Divine Farmer race.

The scales on the bodies of these women flickered with a pinch of dark gold light. Their radiant faces reflected hints of vigilance as if they were on guard against them.

Their formation was not just a coincidence, but was intentional. Their positions formed the Six Snake Shadows Array of the Pear Hill. They were exactly the Six Snake Shadows.

The Six Snake Shadows had made a name for themselves in the Source World. The Pear Hill would handpick only the most exceptional talents from each generation of the Snake Goddess race and recruit them. They would then offer them rigorous training to become a part of the Six Snake Shadows.

Accompanying Yan, the Six Snake Shadows were given two missions to carry out in the Chaotic Source World: they were to reach the Chaotic Source Realm, and they had to protect Yan at all costs. Even though Yan's strength was on par with the geniuses from other super forces, they still didn't want to take any chances. For Pear Hill, Yan was an invaluable treasure.

Yan turned back. Her face was robbed of all emotions, as she glared at those of the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race with piercing eyes.

"How dare you!" She asked Khalid.

"Who are you to stop us? If it bothers you so much, why don't you join him too?" Khalid retorted while furrowing his brows.

The sudden appearance of the warriors from Pear Hill forced the people of the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race to stay on guard. Even with their empowering presence, it wasn't enough to make them retreat.

However, the situation would now become extremely troublesome.

Mount watched all this unravel from a distance and frowned.

Normally he would not back away from a fight against the people from Pear Hill or the Oneness Sky Palace, but the situation demanded otherwise.

Mount didn't agree with the timing and place of this issue. Moreover, he had a hunch that something was wrong with this place.

The sculptures inside the cave gave off an eerie vibe. Furthermore, the location of the Chaotic Source Spirits was still unknown. Even if they somehow defeated the enemy in time, there would always be a chance of someone taking advantage of their preoccupation and stealing the Chaotic Source Spirits for themselves.

Yan kept her unfaltering gaze at Khalid. Her lusciously long black hair fluttered in the air as a trace of red light enveloped her, responding to her rage. "This place isn't ideal for a fight. But, if you're asking for it, we won't hold back."

As if to solidify her statement, the bodies of the Six Snake Shadows began to glow with cyan color. The Other Shore Power inside other people from the Snake Goddess race began to surge as they activated it.

Khalid never expected such a little girl to hold that much authority over the others. Of course, he didn't want to act on impulse and run into a battle blindly without considering the aftereffects.

During the intense exchange of provoking statements, Mount walked over to Khalid and placed his hands on his shoulder.

"Our primary goal right now is to find those Chaotic Source Spirits. This isn't the time to wage unnecessary battles."

Khalid was a powerful warrior thus pride came as second nature to him. He wouldn't just sit around and gulp down the bitter juice of defeat, especially not at the hands of these women of Pear Hill. If Yan continued with her threats, he would probably be provoked into fighting them head-on.

Mount was familiar with Khalid's temperament. Fearing Khalid would act impulsively, he walked over to him to calm his nerves down.

Khalid clenched his fists as he glared at Zen and Yan before he turned to leave.

But, just as he turned back, his long spear suddenly moved. At the same time, a skull emerged out of nowhere in his hand. He clasped the white spear in his hand and charged in Zen and Yan's direction with determined eyes.

"Devil Soul-sucking Spear!"

As he chanted the words, a light with a mixture of black and gray shot out from the tip of the spear.

Khalid's surprise attack shocked both the people of the Oneness Sky Palace and the Pear Hill. The energy surging from his move was unbelievably strong.

The light seemed to hold a mysterious kind of power. Even the people of the Bearing race and Divine Farmer race were taken aback by it. Mount had mixed expressions on his face. He was annoyed that Khalid had shunned his advice, but he was also surprised at how fast he moved.

Khalid's attack seemed simple, but he had been planning for this moment for a long time.

Yan and Zen were the two most important figures of the Pear Hill and the Oneness Sky Palace, respectively. If they were killed, the others wouldn't pose as much of a challenge.

His Devil Soul-sucking Spear was formidable. It could one-shot any opponent.

The light passed by like a flash. It bypassed many people, including the Six Snake Shadows and went towards its two targets, Yan and Zen.

Before the Six Snake Shadows even had the time to react, it had already reached Yan.

Yan was strong, but she didn't expect this to happen at all. She had pinned Khalid to be a coward who could only throw empty threats and do nothing more.

Just as he sensed the unique energy emanating from the light, Zen became serious.

Fortunately, his Civilization Artifact was activated. As soon as he focused hard, an emerald-like feather emerged and floated in the space above him.

Remaining quick on his feet, he grabbed Yan, turned around and ran with her to avoid the light.

With a whoosh, the light brushed past Zen, making slight contact with his clothes.

As a result, the fiber of the clothes on his back began to rot. The skin directly beneath the fabric turned a charred-black color.

Even though the light shot from the spear was free of poison, the spear itself was a manifestation of pure evil. The light contained a strong power capable of corrosion.

Luckily, Zen's body was resilient against such energy. If he were an ordinary human being, he would not have survived! "Go to hell! I'll make you regret this when I'm through with you!"

Zen was fuming with rage. They had stepped over his last nerve that kept him sane.

He had been wanting to teach the people from the Bearing race, the Divine Farmer race, the New Moon race and the Sun Crow race a lesson.

But he shared the same thoughts as Mount. This was not the right place for a fight. However, he had planned to pay them back for the past with interest once they were outside.

But now, the circumstances had changed. Khalid had declared war when he first aimed at Yan. Yan's safety was Zen's biggest concern. If anyone threatened it, Zen would make sure they didn't live to make the same mistake twice.

"Swoosh!"

All of a sudden, Zen dashed towards Khalid with agility. It was hard to keep track of his movements. It was as if he was a ghost.

Seeing his assault had failed, Khalid realized he misjudged the limits of Zen's capabilities.

The skill Zen had used to dodge his strike was beyond his comprehension.

From his perspective, there was no one in the same level of the Other Shore Realm in the Source World who could have survived that attack.

He had been so sure that he wouldn't miss his target.

However, with a single twist of his body, Zen had made a mockery out of it.

Before he could retrieve his spear to defend himself, Zen had already approached him.

Judging by the situation Khalid was in, it wouldn't be wise to retreat. He decided to take the risk and remain where he stood. The skull in his right hand began to rattle in response to his ordeal. At the same time, a solid beam of brown light swirled around the tip of the spear.

He was planning to retaliate with a more powerful strike than before! Watching Zen close the distance between himself and them, Mount and Mya took caution to the situation and became serious.

They blamed Khalid in their hearts for provoking an avoidable scenario because of his impulse. Even so, they had to do something to stop Zen.

If Khalid were to die, the Bearing race would suffer an incalculable loss.

They couldn't just stand by and let this happen.

"Boom!"

Mount's body underwent violent tremors, and then a layer of gold light surged out of his tanned skin. The outburst of energy from his body resembled that of a sturdy mountain.

On the other hand, Mya ascended to the sky and stationed herself behind Mount. A loud cracking sound of bones resounded in the air around her as her right hand broke itself.

From the joint of her elbow, a small puppet emerged as it floated above it. It was her Other Shore Token. The puppet appeared to have been connected to her body with her forearm. Its appearance was nothing short of creepy.

Zen showed no signs of hesitation even though he knew he would have to take on all three of them at once. He was determined to tear Khalid into pieces no matter the circumstances.

Before the both sides could confront each other, the eyes of the sculptures in the cave suddenly opened.

Chapter 3405 The Purpose The moment those huge eyes opened, everyone in the cave felt as if their hearts were clenched in an icy grip. They quavered in fear.

Some of them could feel a sharp sword pointed at their foreheads. If the sword were to be thrust one inch closer, it would pierce their skulls and they would die.

Some of the people in the cave could see they were surrounded by skeletons. This was frightening. Had they arrived in the death world, where no living being existed? Were they doomed to become like the skeletons? Most of them covered their heads with their hands, horrified. Naturally, they thought they were going to die.

Although most of them had been through many dangers, now, they were terror-stricken. Each of them felt like they were at death's door, knocking loudly.

Even Zen and Khalid, possessing the powerful Souls of Light, were not immune to this fear. Zen had to retreat after he landed, and at the same time fight against the fear of the Dreaded Eye Demon with his strong will.

Zen had gone through something like this before in the Sacred Mallow Temple. At that time, after No. 9527 prompted him, he was able to shut it out using the Emotion Closing Godly Way.

However, the fear which descended on him now was many times stronger than what he encountered in the Sacred Mallow Temple. The Emotion Closing Godly Way was unable to banish the fright.

"Flow Strike!"

Desperate for a solution, Zen pulled out another one of his skillsâ€”the Flow Swordsmanship.

The Flow Strike was regarded as an extension of the Emotion Closing Godly Way, with a meditation component. It was a more effective way of cultivating the heart.

While staying in the Flow Sword Sect, Zen had come a long way as far as his training went.

But the mind method of the Flow Swordsmanship had little effect on that fear. He was unable to completely erase it.

The others were even worse.

Most of them prostrated themselves on the ground. Some of them were looking ashen, some were trembling and the rest were crying bitterly.

Yan stood still with a confused look, as if she were also using some kind of mental method to filter out the fear.

At the top of the main peak, the dark and red lights continued to flicker on the surface of the giant eye.

The giant eye was the source of the fear, naturally emanating it and affecting everyone.

Both Zen and Khalid were targets chosen by the eye and the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits. It did not want anything to go wrong in the fight between those two.

However, Khalid reacted recklessly. When the battle began, the giant eye had to interfere.

"What if they find out about your meddling?" asked the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits.

She was afraid they would escape, and leave the Chaotic Source World.

After all, no one was willing to let their prey run away like that.

"There shouldn't be a problem," the giant eye replied. "They haven't acquired enough Chaotic Source Spirits, so they won't put a halt to the competition and take off."

The giant eye wasn't willing to reveal its ability now, but it had no choice.

"Buzz..."

The light in its pupil lasted for 30 seconds before it disappeared and the eye went back to its former condition.

The red and white lights slowly revolved around its pupil.

In the middle of the main peak, many members and disciples from different races, who thought they were on the verge of death, found that the fear had suddenly dissipated, and they stood up with strange expressions.

"What was that?"

"It scared me!"

"I thought I was going to die!"

The fear made people feel like they were taking a walking tour of hell, and they glistened with sweat.

"Uncle Mount, that power of fear is from the Truth of Goodwill and Malice.

But what kind of thing is it? Why could it affect so many people?" Mya asked in confusion.

Mya knew the Truth of Goodwill and Malice very well, as she cultivated it.

After reaching the consummate level of the Truth of Goodwill and Malice, she could also frighten a large number of creatures. If one had a weak soul, they would be frightened to death.

However, for the Souls of Light that had reached the Other Shore, that effect was simply negligible. Ordinary warriors were immune, unless she was able to fuse with a related Other Shore Token, or to cultivate the theurgy of this aspect.

Mount was powerful and smart. As far as Mya was concerned, there was nothing that Mount didn't know.

"That's the Dreaded Eye Demon. It was a mighty ruling force in the past, but the force didn't fare well on the Other Shore and the Dreaded Eye Demons are almost extinct," Mount replied flatly.

"So why is it here?" Mya asked.

In Mya's eyes, both the items and living creatures on the Other Shore should use a medium to descend in the Source World.

The medium was the inner world of a powerful Other Shore Realm warrior.

"I don't know," Mount answered with a frown.

In fact, the Chaotic Source Spirits had already broken with routine and lived in the Chaotic Source World in a special form.

Essentially, the Chaotic Source Spirits were also the creatures of the Other Shore.

Why were the Chaotic Source Spirits different from other creatures on the Other Shore? Every super force had looked into that, but the reason had not been found.

It could be said that it was completely against the truth when the Chaotic Source Spirits lived in a special form like that.

Once they found out why, the strong existences hiding on the Other Shore and the powerful masters of the ruling civilizations would probably be able to return to the Source World, and even the chaos.

After Zen regained consciousness, he just stared at Khalid coldly.

He thought of killing Khalid, but then the fear rose in him. This was not a coincidence.

Knowing this, Zen ventured a guess.

What had just happened was obvious to him now. A Dreaded Eye Demon must be hovering on top of the main peak. That monster was much stronger than the Eye of Will Zen had fused with! "Why did it stop me from killing Khalid? Or did it just stop me from fighting him?"

Zen thought it must be the latter. But why? It was the first time that Khalid had entered the Chaotic Source World. He didn't seem to know anything about that either.

Why would the Dreaded Eye Demon do that? Zen was consumed with figuring this out, and hesitated to act before he did.

He and Yan led the members of the Pear Hill and the Oneness Sky Palace to retreat to the other side, distancing themselves from the members of the Bearing race.

At this time, in another passageway, dozens of tall figures entered. They were from the Separate Abyss race.

The members of this race gathered and formed three teams in the Chaotic Source World. One of the teams encountered the Evil God, while the other two teams banded together and climbed up the main peak.

This time, the trip to the Chaotic Source World was not easy for them, and they were much more cautious as a result. Many Separate Abyss warriors, over a hundred feet tall, looked at the sculptures on the walls and gathered off to one side.

More and more members of different races came into the cave through the passageways around it.

Most were in groups, but there were some warriors who came there alone.

For example, Milo from the Oneness Sky Palace explored the main peak all by himself. He remained in the Chaotic Source World for a long time, and now he finally threw in his lot with Zen and his companions.

"The Chaotic Source Spirits must be hiding in the upper part of the cave!"

"Let's just make our way up and dig them out!"

"Yes, there is no place to hide except the upper part of the main peak!"

When there were more warriors in the cave, it became quite noisy inside.

They talked about the best way to climb the mountain.

As for the members of the Separate Abyss race, they were impetuous. Two of them flew up and shot toward the upper part of the cave with their huge bodies as large as the hills.

However, when the two Separate Abyss warriors just approached the top, they suddenly let out a scream, and fell down, holding their heads in their hands. They formed a huge crater when they smashed into the ground.

Chapter 3406 One Last Chance Everyone directed their gazes to the upper part of the cave. Two eyes-- the Dreaded Eye Demons flickered with red light.

They lingered for a long while before disappearing.

"What's going on?"

"Is that the Malicious Stare?"

"How could it be so powerful?"

The other races that entered the cave later hadn't experienced the soulcrushing fear. When they saw what happened to the two members of the Separate Abyss race, they were all shocked.

"Those are sculptures of the Dreaded Eye Demons!"

"The Malicious Stare is way too powerful. Is there a strong Dreaded Eye Demon in the main peak?"

"Then how can we climb the mountain?"

These people were experienced and knowledgeable. They not only recognized the sculptures on the walls, but also guessed that the main peak was guarded by a Dreaded Eye Demon.

At a loss for what to do, everyone turned to the Snake Goddess race.

Although the Icy Snow Province was open to the public, it was still under the control of the Pear Hill. The other super forces might not know what had happened in the Chaotic Source World, but the people of the Pear Hill must know something.

"What happened in the Chaotic Source World?"

"You should have let us know!"

"Please tell us!"

"If you keep silent, don't blame us for being rude!"

They had been in the Chaotic Source World for such a long time and explored the periphery and the four peaks, but couldn't find many Chaotic Source Spirits. Naturally, they were angry.

Questioned by so many members of the myriad races, the people of the Pear Hill were under a lot of pressure.

No matter how strong they were, they couldn't afford to anger that many people.

At this time, Yan walked out at a casual pace and swept her gaze across the faces of those assembling there. "The Chaotic Source Sea and the Chaotic Source Spirits are already out of control," she said.

Hearing Yan's words, many of the other races had surprise written all over their faces.

Some didn't understand what Yan was talking about, while some let thoughts flash across their minds.

"What do you mean?" someone asked.

"This is the last time the Chaotic Source World opens and the only chance for us to reach the Chaotic Source Realm. If we miss it, we won't get a second chance," Yan replied faintly.

"What?"

"How could that happen?"

"Impossible! The Chaotic Source World has existed for eons. How could this be our last chance?"

The members of the other races were all shocked.

To them, it didn't matter if they couldn't merge with the Chaotic Source Spirits this time. The tickets to the Chaotic Source World were precious to ordinary people, but to these elites of the major races, they were nothing.

If they failed this time, they'd try again. Where there was life, there was hope. In any case, life came first.

Zen's face was also filled with surprise. He asked Yan, "The Chaotic Source Spirits constantly reproduce, don't they?"

Yan blinked her eyes and nodded. "Yes, but since they're from the Other Shore, their bodies are left there."

In the past, the Chaotic Source Spirits were strictly controlled on the Other Shore, and the place where they were controlled was the Chaotic Source Sea.

Even if all the two hundred thousand Chaotic Source Spirits were killed, the Chaotic Source World would be prosperous again, as long as the strong warriors went to the Chaotic Source Sea and chose several other Chaotic Source Spirits as parents.

But now, after the Chaotic Source Sea on the Other Shore had been occupied, there were no more parents.

Once a Chaotic Source Spirit was merged, there was one less existing in the Source World.

After hearing Yan's words, many of the races were excited. They had one last chance to reach the Chaotic Source Realm.

"What happened in the main peak? Why are there sculptures of the Dreaded Eye Demons here?" asked a member of the Celestial Wolf race.

Yan shook her head and said, "I don't know either. Put simply, if you want to reach the Chaotic Source Realm, you have to go all-out."

Mount, Mya and the talented disciples of the various races wouldn't miss this chance. If they did miss that chance, it would be worse than death. That meant they'd never reach the Chaotic Source Realm, no matter how long they lived.

Yan's words sobered them up, and spurred a veritable brainstorm. They came up with many ideas.

Originally, everyone was on edge, each race not trusting the others. But now, they were in a better mood. They were focused on a common goal.

At this time, another figure appeared at an entrance of the cave.

As soon as it appeared, an invisible malicious aura spread out like a giant beast baring its teeth and claws.

Everyone looked over and found the young man in black standing at the cave entrance. Their faces sank.

"Evil God! How dare you show up here?"

A man in golden armor from the Separate Abyss race took two steps forward, one golden hammer in each hand, and his face was full of anger.

His clansmen also stepped forward and formed a half moon shape, presenting a united front against the Evil God.

They had never suffered such an egregious loss before.

Nearly a third of their clansmen were slain by a young man. This was an affront that demanded blood for blood.

When the other races saw the Evil God, they also looked at him with hatred in their eyes.

After the Evil God entered the Chaotic Source World, he had already provoked many races by killing their clansmen for no reason.

He did the same on the Other Shore.

Even the super forces like the Bearing race and the Separate Abyss race could not escape his hatred.

Someone had said that he would tear the Evil God limb from limb if he found him in the Source World, but the Evil God's power was undiminished in the Source World.

Now that the Evil God was outnumbered, the people assembling in the cave were not afraid of him.

They were all elites of the major races. They didn't believe that the Evil God could resist all of them alone.

There was an indifferent smile on the Evil God's face. The Ways-blending Energy gathered slowly in his right hand and coalesced into a diamondshaped gem, which glinted evilly. Even facing so many strong warriors, he remained calm.

Some of the creatures looking at him were very nervous. What was he playing at? Seeing the restless members of the Separate Abyss race about to rush forward, Khalid of the Bearing race reminded them, "Hamzah! If we fight here, we will risk activating the Malicious Stare!"

Hamzah was one of the strongest of the Separate Abyss race.

Although he didn't want to fight the Evil God, the Separate Abyss race had been humiliated. So he had to fight.

"Really?" Hearing Khalid's words, Hamzah frowned.

"We've already been through this." Khalid cupped his hands and told Hamzah what happened just now.

The members of the Separate Abyss race were arrogant. They didn't hang out with the Bearing race.

However, Khalid still hoped they could form an alliance with the Separate Abyss race. He warned them kindly because he wanted them on his side.

After thinking it over, Hamzah stared ferociously at the Evil God and led his clansmen to the side.

Everyone could see a fight between the Separate Abyss race and the Evil God was brewing.

Chapter 3407 Shut Up The Evil God emerged from the passageway, greeting Zen with a smug smile.

Zen faced this creation of his with a look of indifference.

The Evil God was a creature born from his inner world so it was only a given that Zen knew everything about him.

From his birth to his growth, Zen knew every single detail.

All the information would gather together in his mind with only a single thought.

"You've made a big mistake," Zen hissed.

His creation merely continued smiling at him. "What is it?"

"You should've never used Dorothy to provoke me!" Zen snarled with white-hot rage.

Dorothy couldn't help but purse her lips.

She had fought with this creation of Zen's before and knew very well how terrifying he was.

The Evil God had chosen to spare her life at the last moment and Dorothy caught on pretty quickly as to why: he wanted to use her to provoke Zen.

She trusted Zen's strength wholeheartedly, but she didn't want him to get into this potentially dangerous fight just because of her. Moreover, the current situation was skewed to the Evil God's favor.

If Zen was defeated by the Evil God, he would only end in death.

It was nice to be saved by Zen but she wasn't as relieved as she should be.

In fact, she was very worried.

Zen was wholly determined to fight for her and would not back down from this fight with the Evil God.

It warmed her heart but it was quickly overtaken with worry for Zen's life.

"Tsk, tsk, tsk..." The Evil God shook his head with a smile. "You seem really eager to destroy me."

"You never should've existed in the first place," Zen countered.

This creation of his was a freak and Zen was still at a loss as to how such a vile creature appeared in his inner world. Other people didn't seem to have this problem. Why him? Did it have anything to do with the primitive land? The Evil God let out a maniacal laugh. "My existence wasn't decided by you. Not even this round of chaos can decide my birth. I am destined to transcend everything while you..."

He paused to glare at Zen with his two evil eyes. "You are merely destined to be my stepping stone."

His daring insults caused the various races to frown.

There was truly no limit to the Evil God's arrogance.

Destined to transcend everything? Even if he came from the Black Ship, he was not qualified to say something like that.

What in the world made him so confident to say those words? "Shut up!"

Yan shouted in frustration.

Her yell seemed to hold some power as light suddenly shot out from her and towards the Evil God at shockingly fast speed.

It was the Words Spirit nurtured by Yan! The Truth of Holy Words was a very special type of Truth of Godly Way.

Only a few people were suited to cultivating it, even in the Source World.

Yan was one of these few people and was even regarded as one of the best in cultivating the Truth of Holy Words.

Upon reaching the consummate level of the Truth of Holy Words, a warrior would then gain the ability to form their own Words Spirits.

These Words Spirits were then nurtured, cared for so that they grew strong.

Yan had been greatly favored by the Snake Goddess on Pear Hill. When Fuxi arrived, she managed to gain the guidance of two able masters and strengthened her Words Spirit to an unimaginable level.

Despite this, however, Yan did not use it that often.

Powerful Words Spirits could kill people with a single word from their masters.

The more powerful ones were even said to make words come true, words that had the ability to change the course of destiny.

This sudden move from Yan caught the Evil God by surprise. As soon as she said "shut up," the Words Spirit came at him and sewed his lips shut.

"You are a mere secondary creature from my brother's inner world and that's all you will ever be. Do you really think those people from the Black Ship can make you invincible? The world isn't anything that a secondary creature like you could ever imagine..."

Yan lashed out this bitter, cruel truth in the Evil God's silence.

She could see him thrash, trying to refute all that she said, but he couldn't, not when her Words Spirit attacked him like that.

He was too proud, too arrogant, and not just to his enemies. He treated even those from the Black Ship like Shera as nothing more than dirt underneath his shoe.

Anyone who dared speak against him was dealt with ruthlessly.

Yan, however, could care less. She mocked him nonstop and the Evil God's face progressively got redder in rage. A killing intent surged from his body as he poised himself for an attack.

However, as soon as the killing intent burst out of him, a demon red light flashed above his head.

There was no way he would be allowed to kill in here. Yan was the chosen one by the giant eye. It measured the Evil God's strength and prevented him from attacking her.

At that moment, the Evil God's body was engulfed with ice-cold fear.

Despite feigning invincibility, the Evil God had weaknesses in his soul, much like everyone else.

As this overwhelming power of fear escalated, his body began to weigh him down and his face contorted in pain.

That said though, he still had a far stronger pain threshold than any normal warrior. Despite being in great pain, he continued to resist this power that had taken over him.

"Step back, Yan," Zen warned, standing in front of his sister protectively.

"I'm not afraid of him," she protested.

Yan wanted to prove to him that she was strong enough to take care of herself.

Meanwhile, the Evil God continued to fight off the power of fear, his face muscles twitching as he did so.

He looked ferociously grotesque as he used the soul force to resist.

This horrifying scene shocked the members of the Separate Abyss race, the Bearing race, and the Divine Farmer race.

They too had suffered a lot after encountering the power of fear released by the Dreaded Eye Demon and knew just how horrible it was.

It didn't physically hurt but the pressure on one's mind was overwhelming.

Even Zen was surprised at how hard the Evil God resisted.

Back when Zen was engulfed with the maximum power of fear emanating from a hundred or so sculptures, he shared the overwhelming pressure with the Bearing race, the Divine Farmer race, the Pear Hill, and others. Even so, it proved to be extremely difficult even with the use of the Flow Swordsmanship.

Only a dozen sculptures were activated this time but it should be noted that the Evil God was taking it all by himself. This proved the incredible strength of his soul force.

Zen was definitely not going to let him do whatever he wanted outside the Chaotic Source World.

In fact, he was even more determined to put him right back into his inner world where he belonged.

They weren't the only ones astonished by this display of resilience. Even the giant eye on top of the cave was shocked. "Interesting! Interesting... Here comes another incredible talent, someone who can resist my power of fear!"

"Resist your power of fear?" the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits asked. "If you can't subdue him then wouldn't that mean trouble for us?"

For the past ten years, the Chaotic Source Spirits had been growing in power by devouring each other, as intended by the mother.

However, they all relied on the giant eye.

If it turned out that not even the giant eye could suppress the Evil God, then that was definitely going to be bad for them, which made the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits quite concerned.

"Humph!" the giant eye snorted in disdain through consciousness as the red light shone brighter.

More and more sculptures were activated, releasing waves upon waves of power of fear. All of it was directed at the Evil God, and even the people who were very close to the Evil God were not affected at all.

Chapter 3408 Break The Main Peak Boom! The force of fear swept like tidal waves over the Evil God.

As the Evil God struggled, bombarded by the full force of fear, his face twisted with pain and terror.

The force of fear was a special form of soul attack. Even the strongest souls had flawed hearts, and the force inevitably found the flaw and used it to release all the fear in their hearts.

Despite the rapid increase in the force of fear that attacked him, the Evil God managed to hold on for several seconds before he collapsed onto the ground.

The relationship between the races in the cave was a little complicated, but they all had one thing in common. Everyone hated the Evil God to the core.

Thus, the sight of the Evil God falling to the ground should have made them clap their hands and cheer. On the contrary, however, everyone was silent.

Some looked solemn, while others wore expressions of deep wariness.

The Evil God had a powerful soul, but he couldn't resist the force of fear.

How could they reach the upper part of the main peak? After a while, the red light vanished.

Being punished by the force of fear, the Evil God finally calmed down after managing to stand up.

He said nothing, but his face was etched with grimness. He looked around him with eyes filled with suspicion and doubt.

The Evil God had seldom been beaten since he entered the Source World.

He did not know who had employed the force of fear, but he vowed that he would find out and take his revenge.

"The force of fear is so strong. We are no match for whoever employed it.

How can we continue to climb up?" someone asked in a worried tone.

Mount replied, "Even if we manage to climb up, we will find it difficult to defeat those Chaotic Source Spirits if we are suppressed by the force of fear."

The main peak was very dangerous to climb, even without taking any other factors into considerations. They also had the Chaotic Source Spirits to contend with. After these spirits swallowed each other, their strength increased significantly, and they posed a huge risk for anyone who dared to climb the main peak.

"We can't return empty-handed," someone said gloomily.

Everyone fell silent, wondering what would be the best course of action.

Yan had said that if they missed this opportunity, it would be impossible for any of them to reach the Chaotic Source Realm in the future.

No one was willing to turn back at this point without anything to show for it.

As they discussed the matter, they were interrupted by a sharp, cracking sound.

They looked up. The sound was coming from the top of the cave.

The sculptures on the roof of the cave seemed to have gotten loose, and cracks had appeared on the surface. Three staircases extended down from where the cracks had appeared.

The base of one of the staircases was right next to the huddled disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace. Zen quickly went to the staircase and took a few steps up. He peered towards the top of the staircase, trying to see what lay ahead.

But it was dark and shadowed. No one could see what was there.

Like Zen, everyone else was craning their necks, trying to get a look at the top of the stairs. However, no one but Zen had dared to place a foot on the steps. They weren't willing to risk facing whatever was up there.

While they could only see darkness, they correctly sensed that some great danger lay in wait.

Everyone present was well-versed in the nature and tactics of fighting.

While they didn't know what exactly the Chaotic Source Spirits were thinking, they could just imagine what they would suffer if they rashly marched up unprepared for what they were about to face.

The Evil God immediately knew what everyone was thinking. He stood still, looking around with a mocking smile. He said to everyone through his life vitality, "Like the rest of you, I don't know what's up there, but since they have invited us, it won't be difficult to find out."

Zen, Mya, Khalid, Hamzah and the others frowned. Mya stepped towards the Evil God and said in a low voice, "How can you say that after you were tortured by the force of fear?"

Mya and the rest of them knew how to fight visible enemies. They could defeat them effortlessly.

After all, they all had powerful Other Shore Tokens. Even if they encountered stronger masters at the Other Shore Realm, they still had a fair chance to win any battle.

For example, the Evil God was powerful, but when the four members of the Separate Abyss race fought him together, he succumbed under their combined strength. This was the magic of the Other Shore Tokens. If their abilities were combined perfectly, the power released would be increased tenfold or even a hundredfold.

But the top of the main peak held an enemy whose power was completely unfamiliar to them. The one attack they were sure to face, the force of fear, was something they couldn't resist. They were certain that if they went up right now, they would just end up getting killed.

"If you think it's too dangerous to go up from here, maybe we can go up on the outside," the Evil God suggested.

Most of the warriors here were more used to following orders than thinking outside the box. They wanted to break through inside the main peak.

In fact, there was another way up. They could fly to the top of the main peak outside.

At the Evil God's suggestion, many began nodding in agreement.

"The hurricane outside is very strong," Mya objected.

The Evil God glanced at Mya and asked, "Haven't you ever dug holes in the ground?"

Many creatures present had dug holes all the way from the edge of the Chaotic Source World, so they naturally understood what the Evil God was trying to say.

"Let's get out of here," Khalid proposed.

This time, even more people nodded vigorously. The Evil God's plan was better than the alternative. They were prepared to do as they were told.

In order to get the Chaotic Source Spirits, all of them had formed a temporary, tenuous alliance with each other, forming one large and unified group.

The Evil God laughed. "But there is another way! It is more simple, and it is the one I prefer."

Everyone, including Zen, stared at the Evil God in puzzlement and exasperation. They wondered what trick he was playing now.

"The main peak is very long and narrow in diameter. It's high, but not very bulky, so if we work together, we might be able to break it. What do you think?" the Evil God asked slyly.

Everyone began speaking at once, looking surprised at the Evil God's solution. "Break the main peak?"

"What a bold idea! Do the people of the Pear Hill agree?"

"As they said, this is the last time the Chaotic Source World opens, and there will be no Chaotic Source Spirits in the future. Who cares if we break the main peak?"

They quickly grasped that getting to the top from the outside was only a slightly better choice than just going up the stairs. In either case, they would still be passively entering an unknown situation.

It was definitely a much better choice to break the main peak directly.

Everyone turned to look questioningly at the people of the Pear Hill. Before Yan could speak, Natalie said with a shrug, "Our masters didn't tell us specifically what to do. They let us play it by ear."

Hamzah said, "In that case, we can do as he said. But... I wonder if there is a hurricane outside now?"

He thought breaking the main peak was an excellent plan, but he worried that everyone would just be swept away by the hurricane if they did that.

"Some of my clansmen keep watch outside," said a nonhuman creature covered in something green. "The hurricane will stop at any moment."

Seeing that everyone was eager for action, the Evil God smirked. "Then let's get started. Remember, we only have one chance to do this right."

The Evil God and the others had all been conversing through their life vitality, so the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits and the giant eye at the top couldn't hear them.

The giant eye was narrowed in doubt. Through its consciousness, it said, "What are they waiting for? Why don't they go up the stairs?"

"They are cowards," said the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits contemptuously. Firmly she added, "But they won't give up this opportunity."

At that moment, the pupil of the giant eye suddenly shrank.

"Oh no!"

The scarlet force of fear spiraled in the pupil. However, before it could be released, a violent roar came from below.

The crowd eager to get to the top was comprised of a powerful and diverse group of warriors. Their combined power could not be underestimated.

Most of them could control a level of strength up to one thousand divine megatons. Some could easily control an even greater level of strength, especially those from the Separate Abyss race. By virtue of their perfect bodies, even if they did not reach the Chaotic Source Realm, the strength they exerted was comparable to that of the said realm.

A rumbling sound echoed as the main peak trembled.

A second later, the middle part of the main peak suddenly shook violently, as though it was being torn by an earthquake.

Chapter 3409 Joining Hands For The Moment In the middle of the ring-shaped mountain range, some creatures had gathered in the arrays surrounding the main peak.

Not wanting to risk their lives, they didn't dare step outside of the arrays.

At least within the arrays, they could seek some shelter from the terrible hurricane.

"Such strength!"

They have to come inside if they want to take the Chaotic Source Spirits!" The giant eye reassured the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits through its consciousness.

After the collapse of the main peak, the force of fear that restrained people also disappeared.

All the races grew even more cautious. Besides, they couldn't lower their guard against the Evil God.

Zen stood in front of the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace and the members of the Snake Goddess race. In his inner world, the Eye of Will, the Strength God Totem and that Civilization Artifact quietly floated.

Everyone seemed to be lost in their own thoughts, trying to figure out what to do next.

Hearing this, the others looked at him, speechless.

She had always hated that guy.

Compared to the others, Yan was not that afraid of the Evil God.

Yan pressed her hands together, seemingly in prayer. Then, the blood-red shadow of the Snake Goddess appeared behind her.

Behind them, many races like the Bearing race, the Sun Crow race, the Divine Farmer race, the Separate Abyss race and the Celestial Wolf race also joined in the attack.

In order to obtain the Chaotic Source Spirits, they had all unanimously decided to cast aside their differences.

Each stream of energy ruthlessly ripped open a piece of flesh of the giant.

Chapter 3410 The Mother Emerged At that moment, the various races broke into gasps when they saw the Chaotic Source Spirits.

Chapter 3411 A Bloody Eye Everyone was on their guard; they were wary not only of the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits, but also of the huge eye.
