"No!" Hamzah screamed.

He quickly ran towards them to help his companions, but it was obviously too late for him to do that now.

In a fit of rage, he activated his power. His skin turned red, as if numerous parasites had bitten him. Then, he poured his majestic power into the body of the Chaotic Source Spirit.

"Bang!"

The Chaotic Source Spirit took Hamzah's heavy blow. It was immediately smashed into the ground and left a crater with a diameter of over three hundred feet in its wake.

The mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits had cultivated all those Chaotic Source Spirits. Generally speaking, they were formed after the Chaotic Source Spirits devoured each other. Naturally, the Chaotic Source Spirits that were eaten supported the bodies of their hosts. It was the reason that the Chaotic Source Spirit was unharmed despite Hamzah's fatal attack! Such a thing didn't just happen to Hamzah.

The members of the Sun Crow race, the Bearing race, and the Celestial Wolf race also encountered the same situation.

Since numerous members from many races were gathered together, they could possibly resist one or two Chaotic Source Spirits.

Yet every time they fought, there would always be a few rays of red light that would flash at them.

It was safe to say that to be affected by such a strong power of fear in times of crisis proved to be fatal.

Many members from various bigger races had lost their lives in an instant.

Even though it was hard to guard oneself against the power of fear, there was still a way to deal with it.

"Ding, ding, ding..."

Milo, who was wrapped in a coir raincoat and carried an invisible long sword in his hand, flew around a Chaotic Source Spirit. He looked like a graceful butterfly.

His long sword turned into the dense sword rain and poured onto the Chaotic Source Spirit's body.

In order to kill the Chaotic Source Spirit, one had to let it bear excessive power and exhaust it until it was extremely fatigued.

So, Milo did that just to consume the Chaotic Source Spirit's strength.

"Watch out, Milo!" one of the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace shouted.

At that exact same moment, a ray of red light was shot towards Milo.

The Chaotic Source Spirit that Milo had been attacking bared its fangs when it saw the red light. It intended to swallow Milo as soon as his mind wasn't functioning well.

As the red light was about to hit Milo, his eyes got glassy and dull, and he lost his consciousness completely.

In this state, the power of fear clearly couldn't affect him at all.

Losing one's consciousness was equivalent to surrendering their life to their opponent.

When Milo's consciousness disappeared, however, he became more agile.

He easily avoided all of the Chaotic Source Spirit's attacks and at the same time, he launched an even fiercer assault against the Chaotic Source Spirit again.

Like Milo, Chaim was able to avoid the power of fear as well.

It had been a long time since he had last used the Living Puppet Chains.

Now, it was time to let the Living Puppet Chains pierce his body once more.

Naturally, Chaim became just like a puppet. It meant that even though he was hit by the power of fear, it wouldn't cause that much damage to him.

The power of fear that the huge eye released was limited. Without the arrangements that were made in the main peak, its ability would be far weaker.

Some members of other races had come up with the effective methods after they suffered losses.

More than ten warriors had died in the beginning, but after they employed such methods, no one was killed since then. All the races did their best to fight with the blood red Chaotic Source Spirits.

"Cluck..."

Eventually, the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits began to get restless.

She had painstakingly cultivated the Chaotic Source Spirits for a long time.

They might be able to hold on for a bit more for now, but they would be defeated sooner or later.

"Bang!"

Suddenly, the mother stepped on the main peak, and then her tall and looming figure jumped upwards.

Her huge body flew in the air like a large mountain, and then shot towards the members of the Oneness Sky Palace.

"Chaim, Milo! Dodge!" Dorothy warned, her face drained of color at the surprise attack.

The members from different races were trapped in a radius of a hundred thousand feet, and the mother of Chaotic Source Spirits was about ten thousand feet tall.

Due to her massive size, she only leapt for a short distance to cover a large area.

Despite Milo and Chaim not being under control, they still fought and maintained their presence of mind. Thus, they were able to dodge on instinct and escaped along the wind when danger came.

"Bang!"

As a result, the mother fell down and left a crater that was one thousand feet wide.

Nevertheless, the huge, ten thousand-foot-tall mother kept moving and attacking within the limited area. Everyone began to feel anxious and stressed.

The warriors who were in fierce battles with the other Chaotic Source Spirits ran away when the attacks were near.

Still, the power of fear descended from time to time and trapped two or three men. Those unlucky warriors were either eaten or crushed by the mother.

Some members of the Oneness Sky Palace, the Snake Goddess race, the Ear Mouse race, the Bearing race, and even the Sun Crow race got attacked as well. Within less than thirty seconds, about thirty warriors had died.

On the other hand, the giant eye was still floating in the sky. It kept on accumulating the red light and releasing it from its pupil.

If the huge eye continued its strikes at such a speed, then it and the mother would be able to kill everyone without much effort.

Of course, they would not kill those most important people.

Just then, the giant eye suddenly sensed two puffs of aura that came from behind it.

With a slight roll, its pupil had moved to the back and was greeted with the sight of Zen and Yan.

"How dare you attack me?!" the giant eye shrieked. It began to release its power of fear, but then a cyan silk cloth appeared in Yan's hand.

The silk cloth looked very exquisite, and had strange patterns on its surface.

As soon as the huge eye released the red light, Yan lightly shook the silk cloth.

The cloth deftly wiped away the power of fear that was shot towards them.

The members of the Pear Hill were already aware of the Dreaded Eye Demon's existence before, so they naturally gave the countermeasure to Yan. It was just that it was not appropriate for her to show this item before, so she only brought it out now.

Chapter 3413 The Braveness Rain The giant eye's pupil shrank in horror upon seeing the cyan light from the silk cloth.

"Buzz!"

The blood red force of fear formed a helix, shooting toward Zen and Yan.

Such force of fear was enough to push ordinary Souls of Light into endless fear until they died in the throes of madness.

Yan, however, showed no fear. She gently waved the cyan silk cloth, which promptly extended up to ten feet in the wind.

As the silk cloth unfurled, it began to spin in front of Yan, forming circles of cyan light.

Splash! The force of fear came into contact with the cyan light. But it evaporated instantly, like snowflakes in the blazing sun.

"The force of fear is indeed strong in some aspects. No matter how strong a man's will is, after all, there would always be something that they are afraid of. However, attacks like that are easy enough to shatter," Yan said calmly.

Some evil and sinister methods were very horrible. But these methods were difficult to use, not because they were not of the right origin.

In such a big world, there were always so many people who wanted to be stronger.

However, those who resorted to vicious means, though powerful, had their limits. To become truly strong warriors, people must find the right way forward.

"Braveness Rain!"

Yan shouted. The cyan light emanating from the silk cloth transformed into cyan raindrops which poured down from the sky, heading straight for the giant eye.

At the sight of the cyan raindrops, the giant eye released panic consciousness again.

Its two abilities, however, wouldn't work this time.

One of them was the Authentic Visual World, which was an auxiliary ability to help it distinguish the enemy's weakness more clearly and see through the illusions of magic arrays. But this ability couldn't help it block the enemy's attacks directly.

The other was the force of fear, which was easily parried by the silk cloth.

This seemingly unremarkable silk cloth was, in fact, a treasure of the Other Shore obtained by the Pear Hill.

True to its name, the silk cloth could summon rain.

There was a rain forest in Stage Twenty-one of the Other Shore, shrouded by cyan rain over the years.

Once the Souls of Light entered the rain forest and the cyan rain touched them, the fear in their hearts would be dispelled.

They would feel a surge of blind confidence and braveness.

Some people would fuse with the cyan rain as an auxiliary Other Shore Token. During critical moments, they would use it to fight against the fear in their hearts so that they would become more valiant.

Yan's silk cloth was made of melted cyan rain.

Zen stood behind the silk cloth, feeling the light of the cyan rain. An irresistible impulse arose in his heart, imbuing him with renewed confidence.

'But this confidence is too unrealistic, ' Zen thought. He circulated the mind method of the Flow Swordsmanship to suppress the effects of the cyan rain.

"Click! Click! Click! Click! Click!"

Although the giant eye flew fast, it couldn't dodge all the tiny water drops.

The cyan rain poured over a large area.

Some of the raindrops made contact with the giant eye. Immediately, a sizzling sound could be heard.

The rain could melt the Dreaded Eye Demon! The giant eye quickly fled in pain.

"Zen, let's go after it!"

Yan touched the center of the silk cloth with her finger and rushed forward swiftly.

Zen also flew up, following suit.

When the main peak was broken, Zen had been at a loss.

He had one Eye of Will, so he knew how powerful the thing was.

But the giant eye at the top of the main peak was more powerful than the Eye of Will he had. If they found no way to expel the force of fear, the giant eye would be an invincible existence for them.

But Yan quietly passed on a message to him, telling him that the Pear Hill had a plan.

Zen felt a warm sense of pride seeing her like this. She was now completely independent.

But because the Chaotic Source Spirits were on the attack, Zen was still worried about her safety and chose to protect her.

Click! Click! Click! As the silk cloth rolled in the wind, cyan raindrops sprinkled everywhere.

Some fell accidentally on several Ear Mice. In an instant, their cowardly nature dissipated and they began charging at the Chaotic Source Spirits.

Continually eroded by the cyan raindrops, the giant eye, originally as clear as a mirror, was now dim and riddled with pits and holes.

Whoosh! The giant eye fled to the other side of the main peak in a bid to avoid the raindrops.

Yan stepped lightly on the surface of the main peak. Then she flew down the side like a storm, countless raindrops at her flanks.

But just as she flipped over, a voice suddenly called out.

"What an interesting thing. I'll take it!"

Swish! A black figure lunged at Yan at a very fast speed.

Yan didn't expect there was a man hiding at the side of the main peak. Her face darkened as she drew the silk cloth closer to her. "Shield!" she spat out.

An invisible light curtain covered her in a flash.

With her current theurgy, Yan could now launch an attack by merely speaking.

One word was enough to protect herself.

It wouldn't be easy for talents at the same level to break the light curtain.

But the black figure was much stronger than Yan's expectations. He reached out a hand emitting countless colors. Then a white light burst out. The light curtain broke, as if it was as fragile as glass.

"You!"

Yan then recognized the man. It was none other than the Evil God.

The Evil God looked at her with a wicked smile.

The force of fear was the biggest obstacle in his way. If the giant eye restrained him, he would find no way to resist.

But he could fix that problem with this silk cloth.

He was determined to rob it from Yan on the spot.

As soon as the Evil God tried to grab the silk cloth, a sword shot out from behind Yan's body. A sharp sword radiance extended and stabbed into the Evil God's palm.

The smirk was wiped off the Evil God's face as the sword light went through his hand. His face darkened.

A ray of colorful light gathered on his palm. It was the Ways-blending Energy! The diamond-shaped Ways-blending Energy had been piled up to more than one hundred and twenty layers by the Evil God. It was extremely powerful and could overpower the Other Shore Tokens from Stage Thirteen.

The Ways-blending Energy, condensed to the extreme, burst instantly when it made contact with the sword radiance. The overwhelming power spread in all directions like a scorching sun, attracting the eyes of many people and even the Chaotic Source Spirits.

Other people would probably be immediately swallowed up by such power.

But Zen was also very familiar with the Ways-blending Energy! The sword attack he had launched was to force the Evil God to retreat.

The instant the Ways-blending Energy burst out, Zen had grabbed one of Yan's hands. Yan, still clutching the silk cloth, was pulled backward to a safer distance.

This would be the first time Zen fought with the Evil God since he released the latter out of his inner world.

Chapter 3414 The Second Flaw The bright scorching sun shone high up in the sky. All of a sudden, it disappeared.

The light that was shining upon Zen a moment ago vanished in an instant.

With that, a strange expression flickered in his eyes.

The Evil God raised his hand gently. The diamond-shaped pieces created from the Ways-blending Energy assembled together and danced upon his palm.

The light of the pieces shimmered. It was a beautiful and splendid thing to behold. However, it was also extremely dangerous.

"I have to thank you for your help. You have given me an opportunity to practice the Ways-blending Energy to this extent," said the Evil God with a wry smile. "As far as I know, there are not a lot of Godly Ways found within common people's inner worlds."

Zen remained silent for a while.

He did not care about the Evil God's words. He was most interested in the Ways-blending Energy instead.

Three thousand was not always the exact number. Different masters had different methods of summarizing Godly Ways.

The three thousand Godly Ways Zen and the Evil God had practiced was summarized by Chiyou.

Both Zen and the Evil God were quite accustomed to using these three thousand Godly Ways.

However, Zen found something unique in the Ways-blending Energy now.

There was a gleam of faint white arc light among the pieces.

But because the white arc light only occupied one three-thousandth of the Ways-blending Energy, Zen could not clearly make sense what it was.

What did the Evil God put into the Ways-blending Energy? The Evil God noticed that Zen was gazing at the Ways-blending Energy.

Seeing this, he broke into an even bigger smile. "Are you wondering why my Ways-blending Energy is so powerful?"

"Yes," Zen replied with all honesty. He was really intrigued by what he saw.

"It's because the three thousand Godly Ways you pride yourself in are flawed. Hahaha..." The Evil God laughed wildly and continued, "Today I will show you something completely extraordinary, so that you may know what the perfect Ways-blending Energy truly is!"

He spread out both of his hands and the diamond-shaped Ways-blending Energy spread like the wings. This display of power was remarkable.

The structure of the Ways-blending Energy was extremely complicated. Its current state was very unpredictable and unstable but it seemed rather mutable. Moreover, the power contained within it was awfully terrifying.

"Yan, retreat!" Zen ordered at once. There was no time to waste.

Yan held the silk cloth with one hand while she made a gesture with the other.

The power of the Ways-blending Energy was indeed terrifying but Yan believed she had the power to withstand it.

Nevertheless, Zen's tone was very serious. Yan pursed her lips but chose to follow her brother's order. Obviously, Zen was concerned for her safety.

Yan was able to sense her brother's emotions very clearly. She knew all too well that Zen wanted to deal with the rebel who came out of his inner world personally. She fully respected Zen's decision to do this on his own.

Whoosh! Yan leapt away from them. She had already put quite some distance between her and the Evil God. Meanwhile, she continued to stare warily at the Evil God and the giant eye that was hiding on the other side of the main peak. She knew she shouldn't let her guard down for even a second.

The giant eye was afraid of the silk cloth. It wouldn't dare to fight back just yet. It remained hidden and unmoving.

As the Evil God gently pushed his hands forward, the diamond-shaped Ways-blending Energy pelted towards Zen like feathers.

Zen remained standing still and didn't bother to dodge the attack.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Several scorching suns exploded around Zen.

As they exploded, they emitted dazzling lights which disappeared in the blink of an eye. Zen merely looked at them and returned his gaze to the Evil God.

There wasn't even a single scratch on Zen after the attack. He was completely unharmed.

"Were you able to see it clearly? Hahaha!" The Evil God laughed once again and said, "Never in your lifetime would you be able to uncover the secret hidden inside it. Don't even bother trying to solve this mystery. I am the only one who can achieve it in this world!"

The members and disciples of the other races heard this while they were fighting against the Chaotic Source Spirits. The Evil God's statement thoroughly baffled them.

They were fully aware that the power of the Ways-blending Energy was strong. But what was the Evil God so proud of? They couldn't quite understand it.

There were a lot of powerful masters in the Source World. Many of them had put a lot of effort in studying the Ways-blending Energy. However, all of them only reached a dead-end. Ultimately, they had no choice but to give up.

They had to admit that the Evil God was powerful. It was just that they didn't have much interest in the Ways-blending Energy. All they wanted to do was merge with the Other Shore Tokens and obtain greater Other Shore Power.

They were not the only ones who thought of it like this.

Through the magic array, the leaders of many large races waiting at the entrance of the Chaotic Source World were able to see clearly what just happened.

Elizabeth frowned at the Evil God's statement. She didn't understand it as well.

Meanwhile, Athemar and Winchell looked grave. The members of the Separate Abyss race and the Bearing race, and the Ear Mice also shared the same sentiment with the two.

"Winchell," Athemar said, "it seems like there is a special energy contained in the Ways-blending Energy of that young man in black." Athemar noticed something while watching Zen through the magic array.

Even though they did not cultivate so many Godly Ways, they had a general understanding of the energies that existed in the whole world. He was quite perplexed at the kind of energy he just observed.

Winchell nodded his head grimly. "Never in my life have I seen such an energy before," he responded.

"Is it the power of some Other Shore Token?" an Ear Mouse speculated as it tried to comprehend it as well.

"The Other Shore Power couldn't be fused so perfectly," Athemar said as he shook his head. "It is truly strange and quite inexplicable."

It seemed like they didn't have a total understanding of the energies after all. The vast majority of people did not know that the original energy of this world was actually incomplete.

Fuxi sat on top of the snowy mountain. As he moved his gaze back from the edge of the Icy Snow Province to the core area of the Chaotic Source World, he also witnessed the scorching suns.

His eyes narrowed slightly when he noticed the white arc light within the energy. Like most of them, he was puzzled too.

"How is that even possible?"

Fuxi had successfully merged three thousand Godly Ways. He also had a better understanding of the Ways-blending Energy than all the leaders gathered at the entrance of the Chaotic Source World.

"Why is there an extra energy? Where does it come from? If I am not mistaken, this didn't exist between heaven and earth in the past," Fuxi wondered out loud. After a while, something dawned upon him. "I see... No wonder the Ways-blending Energy cannot be perfected. Without this energy, they could not be fully merged. Any efforts will be in vain! Now the only question is, where did this guy get this energy?"

Fuxi was absolutely stumped.

Many years ago, people thought that the Ways-blending Energy was the original energy. Once the energy of three thousand Godly Ways was fully merged, even the truth-level theurgies wouldn't be able to match it.

Lots of supreme masters took severe painstaking efforts for countless years to perfect this. Yet, they still failed to merge the energy of three thousand Godly Ways. Finally, Fuxi, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and the others concluded that the Ways-blending Energy was impossible to complete.

The Evil God's gaze was fixed on Zen. He kept watching him as he launched his attack.

He wanted to see the look of astonishment and disbelief on Zen's face.

However, he was completely disappointed. Zen's expression remained impassive. After a while, Zen finally opened his mouth to speak. "If I were you, I would not make this energy public," he said in a calm manner.

"Do you think I'm as cowardly as you are? Don't make me laugh," the Evil God mocked Zen.

"After all, you are not able to complete the Ways-blending Energy either,"

Zen continued as he shook his head. "But because you have exposed this energy now, people will only covet it."

"Haha! I can't complete the Ways-blending Energy?" The Evil God's face broke into a proud smile. "I have already merged two thousand nine hundred and ninety-nine Godly Ways, including this one. I only need the Thunderstorm Godly Way now. I am one step away from completion!"

As the Evil God spoke, he stared arrogantly at Zen. However, there wasn't any sign of admiration or surprise on Zen's face.

Zen retained his calm demeanor. He replied, "Clearly, you have done a great job. Nevertheless, you will never be able to take that final step because the Ways-blending Energy has more than one flaw."

Chapter 3415 The Flaws Of The Chaos It was true that the Evil God had merged more Godly Ways than Zen ever had.

He only needed one more Godly Way to completely finish the cause. It was unbelievable for him to achieve this with his current cultivation base.

If this happened before, Zen probably would have waited before doing anything, just to see what the Godly Ways Great Unity could produce.

However, with the help of the Regal Jade Spirit, Zen had already grasped that the chaos was imperfect.

Among the three flaws, Zen obtained one through the Regal Jade Civilization. He was able to claim the Blood Essence Godly Way, but the remaining two were still a mystery to him.

After his son, Geoffrey, deciphered and interpreted the Sanskrit word formed by blood vitality, he gathered some clues for his search. The Regal Jade Spirit had guessed that one of the flaws stood close to the Element Spirit race, otherwise known as the second civilization. But the exact existence was still unknown.

Little did he know that the Evil God had already gotten a flaw! He also didn't know if the power within the arc light was a gift from the Black Ship to the Evil God or he obtained it from the Other Shore.

The Evil God was a proud, arrogant being, who was very keen on showing the unique energy he had obtained.

For him, Godly Ways Great Unity was just round the corner.

The only thing that bothered him was that his energy had a way of clashing with the Thunderstorm Godly Way.

He attempted over a million times, with no success whatsoever.

He removed the Thunderstorm Godly Way and placed the arc light together with the other Godly Ways. In this way, the three thousand Godly Ways stabilized to his advantage.

The reverse of this also worked wonders. However, the moment the two forces were added to the Godly Ways at the same time, the Ways-blending Energy would collapse.

The arc light proved to be a form of thunder, one that was violent and difficult to control. That was what made it so incompatible with the Thunderstorm Godly Way.

All things considered, the Evil God had tried all methods only to meet failure.

He even attempted to use the Other Shore Power in order to suppress and force the two thunder energies to merge. However, like all of his trials, this failed as well.

What Zen said stunned the Evil God.

"What did you say? There is more than one flaw?" The Evil God gave Zen a look of disbelief.

Those who remained in the Chaotic Source World didn't dare to say a word after Zen spoke. It was met with silence.

After all, they had no business with the Ways-blending Energy. They thought it was not that extraordinary, except Mount, who was not like the others.

In the same moment, the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits was causing a disruption in the area. Anyone who didn't pay attention would be crushed by her.

As everyone ran for their lives, Mount and Mya decided to take action.

Mya's curly hair began to extend to tens of thousands of feet as her face was finally revealed. Her piercing, blue eyes were focused, and she manipulated her hair to wrap itself around the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits.

Even though the mother was much stronger, she couldn't help but be bothered by the messiness of the hair being wrapped around her.

After Mya was able to successfully restrict her movement, Mount began to suppress her.

As he did so, he heard Zen's words despite the noise. He was deep in thought, and his body trembled in surprise. He looked at Zen in pure astonishment.

At the same time, Fuxi, who remained outside the Chaotic Source World, raised his eyebrows. "There is more than one flaw in the Ways-blending Energy? How could this be? If it's true, how many flaws are there?"

If it weren't for the creature that appeared at the edge of the Icy Snow Province, he would have just asked Zen himself.

What puzzled Fuxi even more wasn't the fact that there were more flaws, but that Zen had known it all along.

It was known that three thousand Godly Ways were formed directly through the chaotic energy. The chaos was composed of Dark and Light energies, and these two energies transformed into the five mighty elements. These were the elements that created all things that existed.

In effect, the energy that was constantly divided was considered the internal momentum of the three thousand Godly Ways, otherwise known as the basis to form all chaotic energy.

This meant that if any flaws existed, then the chaotic energy and the chaos would have flaws.

Zen glared at the Evil God, his body pulsing with adrenaline. "Yes," he said.

"There is more than one."

"How did you know that?" the Evil God questioned, doubting the existence of more flaws.

But as much as he wanted to prove Zen was wrong, he knew Zen was not one to lie.

The Evil God discovered the flaw by chance. Having almost died on the Other Shore, he risked his life just to obtain the arc light.

Could it be that Zen had discovered something, too? Perhaps that was where he found other flaws? "But why should I tell you?" Zen taunted.

This was a bust to the Evil God's ego. He narrowed his eyes, and a hint of vengeance flashed in his eyes.

Although he was known to be extremely arrogant in front of Zen, he still had deep reverence for him.

Shera helped him block any contact with the Rebirth Land, keeping him away from Zen's control. However, no matter how hard he tried, he was still a product of Zen's inner world. The fact that Zen was his creator couldn't be ignored.

With that being said, Evil God was determined to know all of Zen's secrets.

"You don't need to tell me anything," the Evil God smirked, "I just have to devour you."

In an instant, the Evil God's aura soared towards Zen.

The turbulent Ways-blending Energy began to spread out, ready to attack. It radiated magnificent colors as it morphed into a diamond-shaped sword.

With the sword in hand, the Evil God charged towards Zen in a swift movement.

"Brother! Watch out!" Yan called out from above.

"It is useless, you fools!" As the Evil God chuckled, he swung his huge sword across the air, leaving a trail of colors before waving it towards Zen's head.

Just then, a red circle of light spread out, and the force of fear from it began to attack the Evil God.

The highly condensed Ways-blending Energy was extremely unstable.

Affected by the force of fear, the Evil God couldn't control the Waysblending Energy. Just like that, it exploded, resembling a huge, blazing sun.

With the amount of energy that had been released, even the Evil God himself would have to suffer if attacked by it. At the expense of his energy, he tried to suppress the fear and flew backward, giving him a chance to dodge.

Yan, with the silk cloth in one hand, gently sprinkled the Braveness Rain across Zen's body to remove the force of fear. "I didn't ask my brother to watch out for you," she mumbled.

The Evil God calmed himself down as much as he could before turning his head.

The eye was restrained by the silk cloth in Yan's hand. He couldn't defeat the eye alone.

He stood no chance against Zen and the force of fear of the eye.

Clenching his teeth, he turned around and dashed to the side of the main peak without another word.

"Brother, must we chase after him?" asked Yan, staring at the black figure that grew smaller the farther it went.

"Do you honestly think that eye will help us?" Zen shot a question back at her, smiling.

"No." Yan shook her head.

"Then we take that eye down first," Zen said.

He was able to slaughter his way across the Chaotic Source World after all, and not just because he depended on the Ways-blending Energy According to the man from the Separate Abyss race, the Evil God had the ability to descend a world but hadn't used such a powerful trump card yet.

The giant eye released its overwhelming power of fear, which was a threat to everyone. Eliminating this threat was the most urgent at the moment.

Meanwhile, Zen was determined to get the arc light in the Evil God's hand.

The giant eye felt extremely depressed.

It let out the force of fear in order to help the Chaotic Source Spirits. On the other hand, this, coupled with the giant sword created from the Evil God's Ways-blending Energy, would no doubt help in getting rid of Zen.

Since there was no way it could take their physical bodies, the giant eye focused on self-preservation instead.

Yan's alertness and willingness to protect Zen came as a complete shock along with the explosion of Evil God's sword strike. Just what in the world was going on? Without any idea what to do and with its hope running out fast, the giant eye turned around and entered the main peak.

Seeing this, Zen promptly changed his direction and threw a punch towards the outer wall of the main peak, creating a big hole from which he and Yan entered.

The place where the giant eye and Zen entered was in the upper part of the main peak.

Multiple traps had been set here previously by the giant eye, along with the engraved sculptures that littered the walls.

As soon as Zen and Yan entered, all of the sculptures' eyes flashed dark red and the giant eye's force of fear surged, enveloping them almost instantly.

Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh...

All around them were glinting, dark red eyes that threatened to subdue them.

"Go mad!"

Zen understood the giant eye's actions. It was no doubt getting desperate.

When the force of fear was amped up to maximum, it had the ability to drown its opponent's mind and disorder their Memory Flame. It could wash away all memories and leave behind a singular emotion: fear. A man who only knew fear was doomed to live in constant, paralyzing paranoia.

The amount of fear that was headed towards their way made Zen pale.

Yan scoffed at this scene. She gently pulled Zen closer as a burst of cyan light from the silk cloth enveloped them, turning into a huge cloak that protected the two.

This silk cloth would protect them no matter what.

"Let me help you," she whispered to her brother's ear.

Staying underneath the silk protection would be inconvenient.

They had to move fast, owing largely to the fact that the Evil God remained a threat over their heads. It would be best to finish this fight with the giant eye as soon as possible.

Zen nodded in understanding. "Okay."

Rays of cyan light appeared on the silk surface as soft Braveness Rain started to pour. Yan pulled the silk cloth off them and let the drops of Braveness Rain wash over them.

With this blessed protection, Zen was able to move fast. He flew in midair and rushed towards the giant eye in breakneck speed! "Stay away from me!"

the giant eye warned through a streak of consciousness. As Zen got closer, it let out a beam of red light that hit him directly.

Despite its attack, Zen remained unharmed due to the protection of Yan's Braveness Rain.

Wasting no time at all, he drew his sword and slammed down.

"Bang!" There was a reverberating sound as his sword hit the giant eye smack at the pupil.

Eyes were the most vulnerable part of any creature, and the Dreaded Eye Demons were no exception.

The only reason they could rule the chaos for a period of time in the past was that no creature dared to look at these Dreaded Eye Demons, or they would risk spending their lives in endless fear.

Zen managed to pierce his sword right into the creature's pupil.

As his sword split its pupil, it scattered, tainting the white of the eye and painting a rather horrible picture to look at.

"Ouch!"

The pain was great and the giant eye simply wanted to roll away to seek refuge into the depths of the main peak.

However, Zen wasn't going to give it that chance! He raised his sword a second time and white sword radiance flickered on the surface of the blade.

Thinking fast, the eye shot a ray of white light towards Zen.

Unfortunately for the giant eye, it did nothing to immobilize the man.

"Nine-Flash Light-splitting!"

Zen's sword radiance flashed as he began to strike hard and fast, cutting the eye multiple times in a span of a short time.

Cuts littered every square inch of the eye's surface.

These cuts healed rapidly but a new one always replaced the ones that closed.

For a while, only the sound of Zen's fury could be heard as he continued this tirade of attacks.

Faced with the reality that it could no longer fight back, the giant eye ceased struggling and stood still, allowing Zen to litter it with cuts.

When he realized that the giant eye no longer fought back, Zen stopped.

He had no idea what kind of existence this giant eye was. If the Eye of Will was a creature from the Other Shore, then the only way it could appear in the Chaotic Source World was if it was an Other Shore Token.

However, if it was an Other Shore Token, who was its bearer? Zen approached the giant eye cautiously and a flash of blood-red light burst out from it all over again. Despite the protection of the Braveness Rain, Zen felt the frightening power of this red beam.

"Is it burning itself?"

An Other Shore Token had the ability to produce a terrifyingly powerful flame.

This powerful flame had its consequences though. It could cause the bearer to die and there was no way an Other Shore Token would do it willingly unless it found no more hope to its situation.

Just as the eye began to burn, the cyan silk cloth from Yan flew and wrapped itself tightly around it.

Zen didn't notice Yan arrive beside him. She picked up the cyan silk cloth and flicked her fingers. "Seal!" With her command, the cyan silk cloth completely sealed the troublesome giant eye.

"I'll give this to the Pear Hill," she told Zen who nodded in understanding.

Yan stretched out a dainty finger and tapped her space ring, sucking the sealed giant eye into it.

One of her established tasks had been to deal with the Dreaded Eye Demon and she had now accomplished it.

The Pear Hill was greatly interested in the eye and Yan will be delivering it to Fuxi.

Had it been anyone else, Zen would never allow them to take this giant eye, but Yan was different. He couldn't refuse her.

With the eye dealt with, they turned their attention back to the deafening roars from outside. The two of them exchanged a nod. "Let's go!"

The bloody lines the giant eye had drawn were now completely gone and everyone could move freely.

Some Chaotic Source Spirits relentlessly hunted down the Ear Mice who, when they could no longer defend themselves, sought refuge in the arrays.

The Chaotic Source Spirits could do nothing as the Ear Mice hid from them.

Several large Chaotic Source Spirits had also broken down, bursting in piles of amber-colored crystals that were immediately grabbed by multiple hands from various races.

Chapter 3417 Snatch In the chaotic situation, another Chaotic Source Spirit fell. As the Chaotic Source Spirits swallowed each other, the one that devoured the others strengthened itself each time.

But they weren't moving all that quickly despite their amazing defensive power. So they could only be moving targets in the face of the outstanding warriors and talents of various races.

A member of the Moon Spirit race was covered with a faint curtain of light.

The light curtain twisted the light, allowing the warrior to hide herself completely.

With that, it was difficult to detect her existence without using spiritual sense.

Her brother was still inside an array. It was too dangerous outside, after all.

This time, she could give him over a hundred Chaotic Source Spirits.

Entering it meant absolute safety. Moreover, no one had sensed her existence in the chaos.

If it weren't for the array's protection, the Separate Abyss man would have killed the boy without hesitation.

In the presence of the super forces, the small races were weaker and did not quite have the right to speak.

On the opposite side...

Clatter...

The sword light shot straight at the Chaotic Source Spirit and hit its back.

Before the Chaotic Source Spirit grew too exhausted, its defense was impregnable.

But its energy could be consumed quickly. If Dorothy struck it a few more times to max out its remaining energy, she could kill it.

Bang! The Iridescent Stone arrived after Dorothy attacked. It hit the back of the Chaotic Source Spirit once again.

Sally's attack was nowhere near as sharp as Dorothy's and Elvinia's, but its frequency was truly intense. The Iridescent Stone naturally disappeared the moment it hit the target and then reappeared in Sally's hand. Once she tossed the stone, it went straight for the Chaotic Source Spirit.

From where she stayed, Elvinia used the Warrior of the Stone Hill to produce countless streaks of blazing sword radiance.

At that moment, Chaim grew rather embarrassed. He had used the Living Puppet Chains again, so now he could only watch from the sidelines and keep the others alert.

Under the warriors' unrelenting attacks, the Chaotic Source Spirit grew tired. Its huge body was dismembered, and the crystals within its body began flowing out onto the ground.

Spotting the amber-colored crystals, everyone was overjoyed.

The Chaotic Source Spirit contained around 2, 000 crystalsâ€”it was no wonder it was so powerful.

The crystals in this Chaotic Source Spirit were enough for about ten people to undergo the Chaotic Source Reinforcement.

When they managed to kill the Chaotic Source Spirit, three figures suddenly swept past them.

They were from the Divine Farmer race. From the way their looks and clothes matched, they seemed to be brothers.

one of them with a mustache called out.

The stone was a mysterious type of Other Shore Token. Once it was activated, it could allow itself and the people around it to enter a unique state where all attacks were rendered useless.

Countless rays of sword radiance pierced through their bodies and shot out.

Chapter 3418 The Energy Levels If the three brothers from the Divine Farmer race entered the magic array, it would be all the Oneness Sky Palace disciples could do to watch them helplessly.

There, they could safely refine the Chaotic Source Spirits and even give the extras to other people of their race.

For a moment, Chaim examined the brothers before continuing, "All the forces in the chaos can be regarded as the flow of energy. But the energy itself can vary from high to low."

Although Chaim wasn't an expert, he knew the different energy levels.

Life vitality was the lowest level of energy. All warriors in the Source World and creatures in the inner worlds could easily use it.

When condensed to its extreme, life vitality became the Godly Way. Its internal momentum then turned into the second level of energy, flowing much faster than the first.

The power of the Other Shore Tokens belonged to the third level of energy â€”the most popular one among masters in the Source World.

But the Other Shore Tokens had all sorts of strange abilities. Those of mysterious type, most especially, could reach higher energy levels. The Shadow Realm wasn't particularly difficult to deflate so long as one could touch or even just affect it. If anyone managed to do so, the realm would perish instantly.

Some Other Shore Tokens could boast about unique abilities, including deflating the Shadow Realm.

Unfortunately, the Oneness Sky Palace disciples present carried no such power. All they could do was watch as the three brothers slowly drifted away.

Now, not only the disciples but also the team leaders at the gate of the Chaotic Source World, including Athemar and Winchell, were angry.

The Chaotic Source Spirits they had just obtained were snatched away by the Divine Farmer race, after all. Of course, they were enraged.

The leader of the Divine Farmer race gave Athemar a mocking smile. This time, ten members of the Divine Farmer race could undergo the Chaotic Source Reinforcement. How could they resist being so smug? Just as the three brothers moved twenty feet away, Zen and Yan came from the other side.

"This brat really thought he could hurt us!"

"How stupid!"

"The disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace are mostly ignorant. Forgive them!"

The trio seemed even prouder than they were before. They didn't seem to be in a rush from the very beginning. Once they saw Zen, they turned around and moved toward him. It was clear that they were trying to provoke him.

"Zen, you can't deflate the Shadow Realm with normal methods," Chaim prompted. "But it is said that the Shadow Realm itself is quite fragile. It can be disturbed fairly easily because the Dark Realm Stone from the temple in Stage Thirteen is of the lowest level."

"So what? You can't destroy the Dark Realm Stone no matter what level it's at," one of the brothers snorted.

Zen's brow raised as a red light flashed in his right eye. He forced fear to rush toward the trio.

"The force of fear?"

"Unbelievable!"

But it still didn't manage to disturb the Shadow Realm. It went right through the trio's bodies.

"The energy levelsâ€¦"

It could break the furnace because its energy level was higher than that of the latter.

The members of several races like the Sun Crow race and the Divine Farmer race were still fighting against the largest Chaotic Source Spirit. It was troublesome killing off any Chaotic Source Spirit, but it was better to go after another one than to waste time there.

The three brothers of the Divine Farmer race were smug at this point. When they walked over before Zen's eyes, the latter gently reached out his hand and conjured a small green cubic crystal onto his palm.

It drew the attention of the trio.

When Zen was at the True God Realm, the crystal was used as a powerful tool to resist enemy attacks.

But Zen didn't have enough blood of the Chaos Ancient God, so he couldn't produce any more Truth Crystals. As a result, the pure power of the Falling Star Palm wasn't quite enough.

The trio had no idea about this Truth Crystal, but they didn't perceive any special kind of power from it. It didn't faze them in the least.

It continued swirling until a ray of green starlight fell over them.

Seeing the power of the Falling Star Palm, Zen smiled bitterly within.

Indeed, it was too weak with the use of only one Truth Crystal.

They definitely hadn't expected Zen to be carrying such a trick under his sleeve.

What did Zen have to do with the Chaos Ancient God? Standing atop the snowy mountain, Fuxi kept his expression calm when he saw the green light from the Falling Star Palm. He had already known about it since he was at the bottom of the chaos.

Chapter 3419 Return The figures of the three brothers from the Divine Farmer race were blurred, which made them look like ghosts floating in the air.

However, it did not pass through their bodies like other people's attacks.

Yet, the blood power could only reach level three. Some weak blood power was at the same energy level as the internal momentum of the Godly Way.

Zen's was different, so what kind of blood did he have? That was only Chaim's guess by instinct, but it was very close to the truth.

But if his memory served him right, it was impossible for many super forces to have such a high level of blood power.

The three brothers were also dumbfounded.

Since Mount appeared when the three brothers were in danger, they became arrogant once again.

Chapter 3420 Ganging Up Ever since the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace had entered the Chaotic Source World, several large races like the Bearing race, Divine Farmer race, and the Sun Crow race had been constantly hostile towards them.

These races had offended Zen many times, but now they just wanted to end the matter so easily.

What Zen had meant was to ask the Divine Farmer race to take out another more than two thousand Chaotic Source Spirits.

The Divine Farmer race, however, also had many members. If he gave their Chaotic Source Spirits to Zen, then there would be ten people in their race who would lose the chance to receive Chaotic Source Reinforcement. It was a big loss for them.

Still, Zen's expression did not change at all.

Everyone was currently seizing the chance to kill the Chaotic Source Spirits, and no one would want to waste time.

Then again, what had been said was like water that had been spilled. If the Divine Farmer race didn't want to pay, then Zen would show no mercy.

Although Yan didn't say anything, she stood beside Zen.

Her brother's enemy would also be her enemy, and she represented the Snake Goddess race.

If Mount fought here, then the Pear Hill would also be automatically involved.

Since it wasn't the right time to think about the matter too much, he made a decision on the spot. With a flip of his hand, the light of his space ring flashed, and the Chaotic Source Spirits in the space ring spilled out and piled up on the ground.

Zen didn't have time to check the number carefully, but he found that the size of the pile was about the same as the pile of crystals the three warriors had returned.

"Let's go," said Mount.

The three warriors were devastated when they saw the pile of Chaotic Source Spirits on the ground, but they could do nothing about it. They could only send death glares across Zen before they finally left.

"This man is a decisive personâ€¦" Chaim said in a low voice as he watched Mount's receding figure.

Zen stepped forward and gently stretched out his hand. An invisible force stuck to all the Chaotic Source Spirits. With a light flick of his finger, all the crystals went into his space ring.

"I will distribute these Chaotic Source Spirits later," he said.

He had intended to let Sally, Hutton and the other Nine Li members enter the arrays first. After all, they were the only outstanding descendants of the Nine Li race left. However, when he thought of the other disciples from the Oneness Sky Palace who might have complaints, he decided to distribute the Chaotic Source Spirits later.

Suddenly, they heard an ear-piercing scream that came from not far away.

Apparently, a Chaotic Source Spirit jumped up and caged two members of the Celestial Wolf race under its feet. Eventually, it pushed itself down and crushed the two warriors into a meaty paste.

In the past, the Chaotic Source World had always been friendly to some small races.

Even if they only wandered around the periphery of the Chaotic Source World, they could dig up a few Chaotic Source Spirits and receive the Chaotic Source Reinforcement.

But this time, all the Chaotic Source Spirits gathered at the main peak, and the cruel side of the game was revealed to everyone.

A Chaotic Source Spirit of that size was prey to a super force like the Oneness Sky Palace. Small races, however, weren't strong enough to kill it.

If they were not careful enough, they would quickly die.

"Let's go and kill it!" Elvinia exclaimed. She took the initiative and immediately flew over to the Chaotic Source Spirit.

The disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace were thrilled when they saw the Chaotic Source Spirit. The way they saw it, it was like about three thousand Chaotic Source Spirits were waving at them.

Zen's and Yan's figures flashed swiftly across the field as they too, charged towards the Chaotic Source Spirit.

Chaotic Source Spirits were tough and had powerful strength, but their speed was their biggest setback--and so, they couldn't resist attacks that came from various kinds of abilities.

If only they were inside the main peak, with the huge eye's help, then no one could probably defeat them. But now that the joint forces of all the warriors had destroyed the main peak and sealed off the giant eye, the Chaotic Source Spirits were far less frightening than they were before.

The Chaotic Source Spirit roared and struggled continuously, but it couldn't hurt any Oneness Sky Palace disciple. It was like a powerful beast that was trapped and cornered to an invisible space by everyone, and the power of many crystals in its body was weakened little by little.

In a span of a minute, the Chaotic Source Spirit let out an ear-splitting roar, then its four limbs flailed in the air before it fell to the ground with a loud thud. Elvinia and Dorothy went forward first. They released two rays of sword radiance that sliced the Chaotic Source Spirit's abdomen, then all the crystals in its body flowed out.

The mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits was over ten thousand feet tall.

From afar, it looked as though the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits was flying a kite, with Mya's hair serving as the kite's thread. The two people on the other end of it flew higher and higher in the wind.

Chapter 3425 Deletion The strong hurricane beat against Mount and Maya harshly, but they continued to fly high.

The mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits attempted to pull the two down, but every time she pulled Mya's hair, her hair grew even longer.

Therefore, it was impossible for the mother to exert any more strength, and naturally she couldn't pull the two down.

"When that part of the space was folded, I exiled him," Mount replied.

Mya pursed her lips and asked again, "It's not difficult to exile someone in the space, and such a method is not fatal, right? Can you kill him?"

Overall, the space in the Source World was stable--the True Gods who cultivated the Space Godly Way could not tear the space apart, and it was also hard for them to exile their opponents. On the other hand, it was easy for the Other Shore Realm warriors who cultivated the Truth of Void Destruction to do the same thing.

Such powerful warriors were also not afraid of being banished from the space. As long as they released enough strength, they could easily destroy the space that imprisoned them and get out of it.

"That's not what I meant," Mount explained patiently. "After I folded the space, it completely disappeared. In fact, that area with the radius of ten feet has been removed entirely from the chaos. Do you understand?"

After a normal space theurgy had torn a part of a space apart, there was still a void left in the space, and the space itself did not disappear.

Besides, the space had a high ductility. It would not take long for the surrounding space to squeeze into the void, and then the space would be repaired gradually.

Sometimes the space was just like water, as it flowed without a stop.

This time, however, Mount directly deleted a piece of space which involved very complicated rules. It was truly difficult for Mya to understand such a matter.

"I don't understand," said Mya with a shrug. As she was still confused, she asked, "He won't come back, right?"

"It's hard to say," Mount responded.

Once again, Mya was speechless in confusion. Of course, she knew how powerful Mount was.

He could kill any opponent in one attack.

The moment Mount chose to launch an attack in the array, Mya knew that Zen was doomed.

"He is not an ordinary person," said Mount.

Mya's eyebrows shot up in surprise upon hearing those words.

He was positively confident in his abilities.

In theory, Zen had already disappeared, but he still refused to tell the others that he had died.

Dorothy didn't expect that Mount possessed such a unique and remarkable ability.

"Sally, don't worry. Let's wait and see. Zen is very extraordinary. He will clearly have a way to return," Hutton consoled her.

The members of the Nine Li race looked up to Zen as their only hope.

Obviously, they didn't want him to be in danger or worse, die.

It was true that Hutton was not as well-informed as the disciples from the Oneness Sky Palace, but he was certain that Zen would definitely come back! In the other array, Yan stood under the light barrier, her dark brown eyes filled with complex emotions. Worry, sadness, and anger mixed together, filling her mind and heart.

"Yan... Your brother will be fine," Natalie comforted her.

Yan had always been a very optimistic girl in the Pear Hill. It was the first time Natalie had seen her look this miserable.

In Yan's eyes, the only possible accident that could happen was involved with the Evil God.

Therefore, she had been on her guard against him.

It was difficult for others to notice the Evil God's presence, but Yan could always vaguely feel his position.

Despite her precautions, the unexpected thing had happened. The strapping young man of the Divine Farmer race had always been low-key, but after he took action, Zen had disappeared. It was hard for Yan to accept the fact for the time being...

What made Yan even more worried was the terrible destructive power of the folded space.

During the process of folding space, that young man even cut off half the hand of the mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits! Was that an ordinary space theurgy? "Phew!"

Five minutes had passed.

Soon enough, the hurricane of the Chaotic Source World slowly stopped.

Thick hair that measured hundreds of thousands of feet long, emitted a faint glow and curled around the mother.

Mya and Mount slowly descended from the dim sky.

At that moment, all of warriors in the core area rushed out of the arrays at once.

The mother of the Chaotic Source Spirits was the last treasure for them to fight for.

If they were in single combat, no one in the core area could defeat the mother, and it would be harder to consume the amber-colored crystals in her body.

Yet, that could change if they attacked her together.

Some of them could grab a hold of the mother and restrict her flexibility, some could hinder her speed, and some could weaken her strength. Those numerous methods when combined together made the mother not so terrifying anymore.

Meanwhile, Khalid took out his long spear as well and charged straight towards the mother.

Although Mount had made Zen disappear, there were still many competitors for him. The Ear Mouse race, the Separate Abyss race, and the other super forces were formidable opponents as well.

Just as Khalid was rushing towards the mother, a petite figure blocked his way.

Chapter 3426 Be Prepared To Die The Pear Hill was a formidable group, and no one ever underestimated them. Yet it still shocked many when Yan was able to blow Khalid away in a single move.

After all, Khalid was the best talent of the Bearing race. Perhaps he had been careless because he underestimated Yan. But it was still difficult to comprehend how easily she had overpowered him.

In the Chaotic Source World, the struggles were fierce between various races, but almost everyone made an effort to avoid facing Mount.

Since the Chaotic Source World had been established, the Pear Hill and other races in the Source World had always followed the rules that had been agreed upon. Chapter 3428 The Gold Abacus Chaim had told Milo that there was only one way to defeat Mount, and that was to stab the latter with his sword.

Chapter 3429 A Black Figure The abacus's beads moved up and down for a while until they settled down and showed the number, one thousand and two hundred.

When Mount saw it, he knew it meant he could only exert six hundred divine megatons of force in the next attack.

Such an amount of force was no longer powerful enough to defeat the talents of the young generation.

Chaim had merged with two Other Shore Tokens. Previously, he had used the Living Puppet Chains several times to transform himself into the puppet of the first Other Shore Token. It allowed his strength to increase exponentially in a short period of time, but the side effect was quite serious.

The second Other Shore Token was the golden abacus.

The origin of the abacus was very bizarre. Chaim once had an adventure in a temple on Stage Nine. Inside the temple, he even found a human! This human was not in the form of the Soul of Light, but existed as a creature of the Other Shore.

Chaim had never heard of human beings living on the Other Shore, so he found it strange.

At the time, the human had been captured by a golden line and would have died from it, had Chaim not undone the hexes in the temple, releasing him.

Chaim simply did so because he was saving someone of his kind.

The human being had been deeply grateful to Chaim. Before he left, he gave Chaim the Other Shore Token, a golden abacus.

At first, he paid the Other Shore Token no mind. His goal was to step into the thirteenth stage of the Other Shore Realm, and his focus was on exploring the temples just to find the soul crystal.

But he soon found the Other Shore Token could be integrated and released at will. Only after he had fused and merged the golden abacus into his body did Chaim discover its use.

The abacus didn't give Chaim strength, but it affected his enemy.

It was not difficult to trigger it. Chaim just needed to land a blow on his opponent.

The abacus used this hit to confirm Mount's strength.

Chapter 3430 The Change Of The World Not only did Mount have a remarkable space theurgy, but also had enough strength to make the Evil God fear him.

Chapter 3431 Copying All The Bloodline Theurgies The shadow of Snake Goddess was a unique bloodline theurgy of the Snake Goddess race.

Chapter 3433 Outside The Chaos Zen was well-accustomed to the Space Law. He had a general understanding of its operation.

Based on his first impression, Zen thought that he must be trapped in some kind of space or within the depths of the space crack.

However, he doubted this as he watched the scene unfolding right in front of his eyes.

Inside his mind, No. 9527 seemed to go blank for a while. Finally, it said, "It's an unknown place."
